Important News Jiangxi Business Community Asks Chairman Chiang to Supervise the Suppression of Communists

The Jiangxi Provincial Federation of Commerce and the Nanchang General Chamber of Commerce telegraphed General Commander Chiang yesterday, saying: "We, Jiangxi, have suffered from communist bandits since the time of Ye Ting and He Long, and their success is due to Zhu De and Mao Zedong. They have secretly grown and spread. Jiangxi is the deepest and most miserable victim. We hereby shed tears of blood and present to Your Excellency a painful statement. Since the great change of the Communist bandits in the 16th and 17th years of the Republic of China, in the winter of that year, they tried to use the poisonous flames in Wan'an, Taihe, and other counties, burning, killing, kidnapping, plundering property, and dividing land. Zhu De and Mao Zedong lurked in the Jinggang Mountains, and the areas of Lianhua, Yongxin, Ninggang, and other areas in western Jiangxi were all miserably poisoned. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, the large army encircled and suppressed the Jinggang Mountains and destroyed their nests, but unfortunately did not annihilate their leaders. Zhu's poison fled from the old nest, running like pigs and wolves, and turning the places they passed into ruins. Their red flames spread from Suichuan to various counties in southern Jiangxi and set up nests in Mopanshan, Donggu, and other places, and used Xingguo and Yudu as the main bases of the red bandits. In the 18th year of the Republic of China, they became even more elusive, running from southern Jiangxi to western Fujian, southern Fujian, and the eastern border of Guangdong, spreading their fierce attacks as if entering a no-man's land. Later, in the spring of this year, they took advantage of the fact that the campaign against the rebels was in full swing and there was no time to look south. The spread of the red flames in the province was a thousand miles a day. Leaders such as Zhu De, Mao Zedong, Peng Dehuai, and Huang Gonglue poisoned the entire province. The division of shares, such as Chen, Lin, Fang, and Shao, poisoned one side. The provincial capital of Nanchang dared to encircle and attack the important town of Jingji twice, and were both captured for more than a month. Eastern Jiangxi was almost covered in red flames, and southern Jiangxi was isolated in one city. Western Jiangxi has long been a den of bandits, and half of northern Jiangxi is in danger. Even Zhangshu, the center of the Gan River, has been miserably ravaged. Some places have been occupied by bandits for many years, and some for a few months. It is difficult to find a clean land for thousands of miles. The areas passed by the red flames are dark, the wind and clouds change color, the houses are in ashes, and the lives of the people are like insects and sand. Everywhere you look, there are broken walls and remnants of corpses. It is heartbreaking to hear the cries of ghosts and gods and the groans of blades. Burning contracts, dividing fields, confiscating property, conscripting men, forcing women, and dividing wives are all that is left to do. The dead are piled up like white bones, and the green phosphorescence is rampant in the wilderness. The living are dying and waiting to die. For example, in Ji'an city alone, the number of people killed in a month has reached more than 10,000, and there are thousands of kidnappings. In Xingguo county alone, more than 20,000 people have been killed in the past month, and thousands have died from being forced to be vanguards and forced to commit suicide. As for the sharing of women, the burning of houses, and the confiscation of property, it is difficult to count them all. From this example, it can be seen that Jiangxi has suffered such a fate. This is truly the brutality of Huang Chao and Zhang Xianzhong's invasion, and there is no such fierce slaughter as in Jiading and Yangzhou, and there is no such long-lasting disaster as in the Guangdong Haifeng and Lufeng, and the red flames in Hubei and Hunan are not so widespread. In this great disaster, the lives of the people are on the verge of extinction. It is a great joy to hear that our Commander-in-Chief's campaign against the rebels has been victorious and that Hebei has been pacified, and it is also fortunate that Lin Shuai's great army has gathered and rushed to Jiangxi to suppress the communists. Our Jiangxi people are coming to Suwang, and there is hope of salvation. How can we make such groans and cause so much trouble? Only by learning from the past and being cautious, are we even more worried. There are many armies suppressing the bandits, but the power of the red bandits is very great. Remembering that when Zhu De and Mao Zedong were driven out of their old nest, there were only a few hundred remnants of guns and a thousand bandits. Now, including Zhu De, Lao Peng, Huang Gonglue, and the small gangs of communists who have fled to Jiangxi, there are about 70,000 to 80,000 rifles, 4,000 to 5,000 Mauser pistols, more than a thousand machine guns, hundreds of cannons, and countless spears of the communist bandits. In the beginning, the government never failed to send troops to track and suppress them. Every time they suppressed them, they always reported victory, and they always reported seizing several guns and killing many bandits, and they always reported recovering a certain place. They also always said that the communist bandits were like fish in a cauldron, vulnerable to attack, and would soon be extinguished. What was the result? There is no need to repeat it. It is not enough to redify the entire Jiangxi, and the poisonous effects have spread to Hunan and Hubei, and even to Sichuan, Anhui, Henan, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Fujian. The momentum of the prairie fire cannot be approached. The future of the party and the country is in deep danger. If the Commander-in-Chief does not personally supervise the encirclement and suppression with the remaining prestige of his divine martial arts, it will be difficult to achieve results. Moreover, if the leader is not captured, the seeds of disaster will be left behind. Once he calls for the ashes to be rekindled, this is even more a matter of concern. Furthermore, what is even more important is that the disaster in Jiangxi is widespread and long-lasting. Farmers and workers have lost their jobs, and all industries are declining. Who will save those who are displaced and homeless? The dead are full of grievances and cannot be诉, and the living have no plan. It is not possible to ask for urgent relief if the country exists, and they will all turn into ditches. Our Commander-in-Chief must be able to coordinate the overall situation and feel sorry for the survivors. On the one hand, he must concentrate the army and personally supervise the encirclement and suppression to eliminate the root of the disaster. On the other hand, he must exempt the people from taxes and all local requisitions and send huge sums of money to save our disaster victims, so that the great disaster can be turned around and the survivors can rely on it. We shed tears of blood and state our words with trepidation, awaiting orders."

Excavation of the Ancient Tan Kingdom City in Shandong

Discovering Black Pottery from 3,000 Years Ago

Jinan Correspondence: The Archaeological Team of the Academia Sinica, in conjunction with the Shandong Provincial Government, formed the Shandong Antiquities Research Association, planning to excavate the old Tan Kingdom in Licheng and the old Qi capital in Linzi. Starting on November 7th, they began excavating the old Tan Kingdom city. Over the past twenty-odd days, significant discoveries have been made. The number of unearthed artifacts has reached over 1,190, totaling over 10,000 pieces. In addition to the antiquities of the old Tan Kingdom (dating back over 2,600 years), they have also discovered black pottery from before the Tan Kingdom. It is determined to be at least from the late Shang Dynasty, dating back over 3,000 years, which is an unexpected and significant contribution to archaeology. I personally went to inspect on the 29th of last month and inquired about the excavation process as follows:

From Jinan to Longshan: I took the Jiaoji Railway train at 8:30 am on the 29th from Jinan Station and arrived at Longshan Station at 9:30 am. I happened to meet a worker hired by the Research Association to dig the city, who led me to Longshan Town, located about two li northeast of the station. Upon arriving at the Research Association's office, I met Mr. Guo Baojun, a surveyor from the Institute of History and Philology of the Academia Sinica, and Mr. Dong Zuobin, an editor. After explaining the purpose of my visit, Mr. Dong and Mr. Guo warmly welcomed me. Mr. Dong had a long conversation with me, detailing the reasons for coming to Shandong to excavate the ancient Tan Kingdom city, the process, the current situation, and the various types of items obtained. The initiation of the excavation: According to Mr. Dong, Wu Jinding (Yu Ming), a Shandong native and archaeologist, is a member of the Academia Sinica and currently a professor at Qilu University. Several years ago, he knew that there were fragments of tiles and bricks from the ancient Tan Kingdom city of the Spring and Autumn period in Longshan Town near Jinan, and reported it in detail to the Academia Sinica. This summer, when the Jin army occupied Jinan, they dug trenches in the area and unearthed many antiquities. The Academia Sinica, recognizing the importance of the discovery, decided to come to Shandong for excavation, first excavating the ancient Tan Kingdom city in Jinan and then excavating the old Qi capital in Linzi next year. Therefore, Chuan Sinian, Li Ji, Dong Zuobin, and Guo Baojun were sent to Shandong to contact the Education Department. After the Education Department submitted the matter to the Provincial Government Standing Committee, it was decided to appoint Wang Xiantang (Director of the Library), Yang Zhensheng (President of Qingdao University), Zhang Dunne (Senior Middle School Principal), and Liu Cixiao (Secretary of the Education Department) as members to join the members of the Academia Sinica to form the Shandong Antiquities Research Association. After the association was established, Chuan Sinian was elected as the chairman, Li Ji as the director of work, and Wang Xiantang as the secretary. An office was set up in Jinan Longshan Town, and excavation began on the 7th in a wheat field, paying the landowner 30 yuan per mu. For those without wheat seedlings, 10 yuan per mu was paid. Currently, 36 workers are hired, divided into five groups, each receiving a daily wage of 4 jiao. Currently, 2,000 yuan has been spent, all paid by the Academia Sinica. The office is mainly managed by Li Ji, Dong Zuobin, Guo Baojun, and Wu Jinding. Attached are eight articles of the regulations of the Antiquities Research Association as follows (Regulations of the Shandong Antiquities Research Association jointly established by the National Academia Sinica and the Shandong Provincial Government (1) Upon the proposal of the National Academia Sinica, the National Academia Sinica and the Shandong Provincial Government shall each appoint two to five members to form the Shandong Antiquities Research Association. (2) The members appointed by the National Academia Sinica shall be recommended by the Institute of History and Philology of the National Academia Sinica. The members appointed by the Shandong Provincial Government shall be recommended by the Education Department of the Shandong Provincial Government. (3) The association shall have one chairman, one director of work, and one secretary, who shall be elected by the members. (4) The work of the association shall be temporarily divided into three steps: investigation, excavation, and research. The National Academia Sinica shall be responsible for the scientific guidance, and the Shandong Provincial Government shall be responsible for the protection. (5) The address of the association shall be set in Jinan, and an office shall be established at the excavation site. (6) The working expenses of the association shall be borne by the National Academia Sinica and the Shandong Provincial Government separately. When necessary, the National Academia Sinica shall bear them exclusively. (7) The antiquities unearthed shall be stored in the association for research. However, for the convenience of research, the association may submit a portion to be studied elsewhere after passing it, but it must be returned to the association within a certain period. (8) The current excavation work is temporarily conducted in Longshan and Linzi as pilot areas.

Achievements of the excavation: Excavation began on November 7th. After entering the ground by one meter, the city wall of the Tan Kingdom was discovered. The wall was 15 meters wide, and the rammed earth traces were clearly visible. There were also tombs built with Han bricks on the city wall, which proves that there were still residents in Tan City during the Han Dynasty. Except for the modern items in the uppermost layer of the ground, no items from after the Han Dynasty have been found below the Tan City wall, which further proves that there have been no residents in the city since the Han Dynasty. Among the cultural items of the Tan Kingdom, the dou (stemmed bowl), li (tripod cauldron), and gui (food vessel) are the most numerous among the pottery, with some being 80% intact. When digging below the Tan City, gray soil was found. In the gray soil, there were black pottery tiles and fragments. The black pottery fragments are the best material for studying Eastern culture, as no items from after the Tan Kingdom have been found in the strata where the black pottery fragments were discovered. This proves that the black pottery is definitely from before the Tan Kingdom. Although there is no time to study it now and its age cannot be determined, it is known that our country first used stone tools, and the Shang Dynasty began to use bronze tools. However, no bronze tools were found in the strata where the black pottery fragments were discovered, which proves that the black pottery fragments are at least contemporary with bronze tools, or even earlier than the Shang Dynasty. We hoped to discover the culture of the Tan Kingdom, but we unexpectedly discovered the culture before the Tan Kingdom, which was beyond our initial expectations. Mr. Dong also showed me the black pottery fragments he had obtained. They were black in color, and the thinner ones were more translucent than Kangxi porcelain. Some also had extremely fine spiral patterns, which were not only antique but also valuable. The precision of ancient Chinese industry was not inferior to modern Europe and America. The items obtained from Tan City and below Tan City have been washed, numbered, and stored. The numbers have now reached 1,193, totaling more than 10,000 pieces, divided into 58 boxes. Among the pottery are dou (stemmed bowl), li (tripod cauldron), and ding (cauldron).

Page 8

·　Dou and li are the most numerous. Among the bronze ware are arrowheads, spring coins, and half-mouth Qi knives. Among the stone tools are stone knives, stone axes, and stone ben (archaic weapon). There are also two pieces of jade. According to research, the latest are from the Han Dynasty. Among the bone tools are bone combs, bone awls, bone needles, and bone arrowheads. The scapula divination tool is even more important than the turtle shell divination tool of the Yin Ruins.

Archaeology of Tan City: Mr. Dong then accompanied me to the excavation site. Leaving the east gate of Longshan Town, there is a river, which is the Wuyuan River recorded in the Commentary on the Water Classic. The towering plateau protruding from the ground on the east bank of the river is Tan City. However, the Water Classic records that the river is east of the city, but now it is west of the city, perhaps due to the passage of time and the changes in mountains and rivers. Stepping onto the plateau, the rammed earth traces of Tan City can be seen. Each layer is about half a foot thick. The locals call this place Goose and Duck City or Chengzihai. There is a small village called Shanchengzi at the southern end of the city. However, according to Mr. Dong, Goose and Duck City was actually in Huantai County during the Six Dynasties. Shanchengzi and Chengzihai are variations of the Tanzi City sound, which is also unknown. The city is 450 meters long and wide, completely a plateau. Looking at Pingling City from afar, it is about two li northeast. The city wall is still higher than the ground, probably because the city has been replaced less. At this time, Li Ji, the director of the Research Association, was measuring, and Mr. Dong led me to the excavation site to inspect.

The situation of the excavation: On this day, Longshan Town held a grand theatrical performance and stopped working without excavation. The excavation site is in the center of the city, dug into north-south longitudinal trenches, each trench 10 meters long and 1 meter wide. The deepest part was dug to 6 meters. Looking down from the trench, the rammed earth traces of the Tan City wall and the gray soil layer where black pottery fragments were unearthed are clearly two sections. The gray soil layer is 6 meters deep, but it is still higher than the plain outside the plateau. The original plan was to dig 45 sections of longitudinal trenches 10 meters long. Now 39 sections have been dug. It is planned to dig another horizontal trench, but due to the cold weather, it was decided to abandon it. Black pottery fragments can be picked up everywhere outside the trench. I also picked up several pieces.

Impressions upon returning: After the inspection, Mr. Dong and I returned to Longshan Town. Mr. Dong said that the association decided to go to Linzi next spring to excavate the Qi capital city and the tombs of the Qi kings, which should yield more complete items. The shortcoming this time is that no characters have been found, but there seem to be symbols and a few characters on various pottery pieces. I also heard people talking in groups of three or five, saying that the Research Association was digging up broken tiles and bricks, what was the use? Some also said that they had dug up a lot of gold and silver, which shows that the villagers are ignorant and only know that gold and silver are treasures. I took the train back to Jinan at 2:00 pm (December 1st).

Shen Honglie Convenes Naval Defense Conference

Qingdao Correspondence: Northeast Navy Commander Shen Honglie has returned to Qingdao this time to strengthen the reorganization of naval fleets, marine corps, and air squadrons. In addition to inspecting the fleets and holding autumn naval exercises in Laoshan Bay last week, he convened the second naval defense conference at the naval headquarters on the 29th. The attendees included Huang Xuxu, director of the Qingdao Office, Gao Fenghua, director of the Yu Ordnance Factory, Zhang Hehuo, commander of the Marine Corps, Captain Huang of the Air Squadron, Ling Xiao, commander of the First Fleet, and the captains of various ships in Qingdao. The internal reorganization and naval defense matters were discussed in detail, which can be roughly divided into four items: (1) Issue orders to various ships to clear out the accumulated bandits on the coastal islands as soon as possible. (2) Take measures to protect coastal fishermen, and severely punish those who disturb fishermen or hinder the livelihoods of island residents. (3) Order the Marine Corps to assist the police in handling public security on land. (4) Reorganize military discipline in various departments, and responsible officers should earnestly admonish their subordinates to uphold military reputation. (December 1st)

Lu Xingbang's Department to be Transferred to Western Fujian Soon

Yan You will be taken over by Liu's Division

Fuzhou Correspondence: Regarding the transfer of Lu Xingbang's department to western Fujian, Chairman Jiang recently sent a telegram to the provincial government, which was forwarded to Lu for compliance, and Chairman Yang repeatedly urged it. Zhou Zhiqun has telegraphed the provincial government, requesting that a team be sent to take over Sha Yong and inquiring about the allocation of military expenses. The telegram stated that the department is preparing to depart for western Fujian in its entirety. However, it is not yet clear whether the supplies will be allocated directly by the province or whether funds will be raised in Beijing. We hope to receive instructions and allocated funds to maintain operations. Although the province has not yet made a decision, Lu seems to have no choice but to lead the First Brigade to set out immediately for western Fujian.

Lu Xingbang was previously concerned that the provincial military preparedness had not been removed, and there would be concerns about the rear once he departed. Although the provincial government quickly ordered all armies to allow passage and telegraphed Lu's army to set out with peace of mind to meet expectations, Lu would have an excuse if the departure fee was not allocated. Chairman Yang has ordered He Gonggan and Chen Peikun to raise funds and remit them to Yan for application.

The defense of Yan You will be filled by a certain department, which is also related to the issue of Lu's department's departure. Recently, there were reports that Liu's division and the Second Brigade would take over the defense. Now, Liu's division has been tasked with filling the defense. On the 28th, Liu Heding specially went to the provincial government to visit Chen Peikun and Yang Tingying, the director of military affairs, to discuss the handover. It is said that concrete measures have been decided. As for the defense of Datian, the provincial government ordered the Minbei Bandit Suppression Advance Team commanded by Chen Guohua to fill the defense, which was announced yesterday. (November 29th)

Wuhu-Hefei Shuttle Boat Robbed

Wuhu Correspondence: Wuhu is the commercial center of Anhui Province, and its transportation is also very important. In addition to Chinese and foreign merchant ships on the Yangtze River, as well as long-distance buses to Jingwu, Guangxuan, etc., small boats operating in various places include Nanjing, Dong'anqing, Datong, Hefei, Chaoxian, Nanling, Xuancheng, etc., which are also very developed in carrying goods and passengers. Unexpectedly, in recent years, southern Anhui, which was once known for its peace, has become a den of bandits, so that all but one small boat to Nanjing have been robbed, and some boats have been robbed several times. Although shipowners have repeatedly appealed to the authorities to take measures to protect them, it is difficult to defend against the numerous bandits in the interior. The other day (29th), the Yuan Bing shuttle boat from Wuhu to Hefei, carrying a tugboat full of passengers and cargo, set off for Hefei. At 7:30 pm, it was sailing on the Qingxikou River, ten miles away from Chaoxian County, when bandits who had been lying in wait on the boat, disguised as passengers, suddenly opened fire, forcing the boat to stop. At the same time, bandits lurking nearby also rowed several boats carrying more than 20 bandits and boarded the shuttle boat, firing shots to intimidate the passengers. As the wind and rain were raging and the sky was dark, the bandits wantonly searched and robbed, first robbing the tugboat and then robbing the passengers on the shuttle boat, even those who had only one or two yuan of silver hidden on them were swept away. The robbery lasted for half an hour before they transported the stolen goods down and rowed away. The total loss is estimated to be 20,000 yuan, and one fireman was beaten and seriously injured. Fortunately, the passengers were unharmed. The boat resumed sailing to Chaoxian County at 9:00 pm. The Chaohu Water Police Bureau reported the incident and immediately dispatched patrol boats to pursue the bandits, but they were nowhere to be found. A few days ago, the Xin Shenglong shuttle boat from Wuhu to Datong was robbed in the Bianxingzhou area, and the second mate was injured. The Sixth District Bandit Suppression Command successively arrested Hu Shengwu, Liu Haiqing, Zheng Haishan, Yu Changqing and other four bandits in Wuhu Ju Zhi'an and other places. They confessed to the robbery of the boat. This morning at 11:00, they were tied up and taken to the 13th Daomen along with Wang Huanzhang, Zhang Yejing, Zhang Rongguang and other seven bandits arrested in the countryside for robbery, and executed by shooting. (December 1st)

Soviet Union Accuses White Russians of Hindering Education Again

Harbin Correspondence: The Russian Consulate in Harbin requested the authorities to ban White Russian political activities in the Northeast a month ago. The authorities ordered the Special Police Department to search the homes of important White Russian leaders several times, but to no avail. The Russian Consulate has not protested again since then. As for the schools for Soviet railway staff children in the Special Zone, they are run entirely by red personnel, and the White Russians have no say in the matter. Unexpectedly, the Soviet side recently suddenly stated that Soviet students are being subjected to reactionary oppression by White Russian youths, which makes school education quite unfree. The Chinese education authorities ignore this and do not ban it. The Moscow government secretly ordered Soviet school teachers along the East Railway line to prepare reports so that its plenipotentiary representative can lodge a protest with our country at the Sino-Russian conference. Currently, various Soviet schools are fabricating facts to make reports.

It is also heard that Moscow will change the highest Far East party organ into the Special Zone Party Department. The party department has the power to handle all party affairs in the Far East, and the cadres are the commanding organ. Also, the headquarters of the Soviet Third International Communist Party currently feels that Shanghai and Liaoning lack talents who are familiar with foreign languages ​​for implementing various plans, and specially ordered the Soviet agencies in Harbin to send party members from the Special Zone Party Department and the Youth Party Department who are proficient in foreign languages ​​to Shanghai and Liaoning for deployment at any time. (November 29th)

Local Correspondence Songjiang

Notorious bandit arrested and executed in Fengjing: Gao Zhongshu, a bandit from Fengjing, had repeatedly committed major kidnapping cases. The authorities had ordered his arrest for a long time but had not succeeded. Last month, Chen Zhankui, the director of the Songshan Fengjing Joint Defense Office, together with the military and police, formed a joint team. Detective Yang Shijie was arrested in Shenjiabang and seized guns and ammunition. He was escorted to the Garrison Command. After interrogation by Battalion Commander Zhang Rubit, the case was reported to the Songhu Garrison Headquarters and approved for execution. After receiving the document, Battalion Commander Zhang sent Detective Yang, a platoon leader, and others to escort the criminal to Fengjing on the 2nd and executed him by shooting at Wenchang Pavilion.

Bandit leader Yao Jinshan arrested in Shanghai: On the 29th of last month, Yao Jinshan, the leader of the kidnapping of the Shen family's young child in Fengjing and other cases, was wandering in front of the Small World. Detective Yang Shijie of the Military and Police Inspection Office and informant Cai Ahai recognized him. They joined the police on duty at the Second Precinct of the First District and arrested him, taking him back to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for custody. Detective Yang has reported to Songjiang that the county government has prepared a document and sent Detective Yang to Shanghai to escort him back for trial according to law.

Suzhou

Young man kidnapped but luckily escapes: Xie Zhenghua, a sixteen-year-old apprentice at Shixin Changhua Cosmetics Store in Guanqian Street, a native of Ganlu, Suzhou, went out of the store to his father Zhou Yongquan's residence at No. 10 Chuanzhu Lane in Changmen Nei the day before yesterday afternoon to pick up winter clothes. Because his family had not yet sent the clothes, Xie turned to the Qian Wanli Ganlu shuttle port outside Pingmen to send a letter urging them. When he arrived, the boat had already left, so he had to enter Pingchuan back to the store. However, when he walked to a remote place behind Beisita Pagoda, two strangers suddenly came forward and stopped Xie, threatening him with a pistol. Xie saw that they were fierce and did not dare to argue with them. He was then taken by the two men out of Pingmen and onto a boat. The bandits took a cup of tea and forced Xie to drink it. Xie fell into a coma after drinking it. The bandits immediately sailed the boat to the vicinity of Guanli outside the Qimu Gate. It was already late at night, so they docked the boat. A bandit asked Xie if his family had money. Xie replied that he was an apprentice, how could he have money? One bandit said not to say much and take him to Shanghai. After a while, a bandit woman took dinner to Xie. Xie couldn't swallow it because he was frightened. When Xie was sleeping, the bandits planned to tie him up, but Xie begged for mercy and was spared. Until midnight, Xie pretended to go to the toilet and got up twice, but was watched by the bandits. On the third time, the bandits were all asleep. Xie then stepped ashore, escaped along the railway, and arrived at Suzhou Station at about 4:00 am yesterday morning. At that time, he was mentally exhausted, so he hired a rickshaw to enter the city and went to his father's place to describe the incident in detail. His family was shocked when they heard about it. It was a dangerous situation.

Escort arrested and jailed for letting prisoner escape: Four judicial policemen from the Yang County Government were ordered to escort two prisoners to Ganzhou Inspection County. When they arrived in Zhongzhou, one prisoner escaped. The four policemen returned to the county to report to the county government. The county magistrate believed that the escape of the prisoner was due to bribery by the judicial police, so he arrested all four policemen. One of the policemen, Ye Changhou, was visited in prison by his younger brother Ye Za, who colluded with his friend Xie Weishu, who secretly carried a hemp rope. During the meeting, he sleeved the rope to the policeman and agreed to nail an iron hook on the toilet outside the prison that night so that the policeman could hang the rope down. That night, he escaped from prison without a trace. It was not until the morning that they discovered the escape. Yesterday, the county magistrate telegraphed the President of the High Court, Lin. After receiving the telegram, President Lin immediately telegraphed the trial officer of Suqian County, Wang Enpei, to investigate and deal with the matter according to law.

Lu Xu Town villagers kidnapped: The other night, four or five bandit ships from the Luhu Township of Wujiang County, led by Little Boss Xi Zhu Luo A Mei under Ah Shu, the Taibao of Pudong, resulted in the kidnapping of two villagers. Yesterday, the district reported the incident to the Water Public Security Third District and requested an investigation. District Chief Shen ordered the 14th team led by Team Leader Xu to go to rescue the hostages. The court requested that opium be used for medicine: Yesterday (2nd), Lin, the President of the High Court, received a petition from Huang Yongzhong, the President of the Zhenjiang District Court, requesting that the opium confiscated by the court be prepared as anti-smoking pills using chemical methods and distributed to the opium prisoners in custody. The reason is that recently there have been reports that many opium prisoners in the Suzhou Third Prison have died of opium addiction. There are also many opium prisoners in prisons in Zhenjiang, Shanghai, and other places. In order to prevent the same opium addiction from causing death, this request is made. Dong Changmin, the warden of the Shanghai Second Prison, also sent a public letter to the Zhenjiang District Court proposing this proposal. After receiving the petition, President Lin said that it should be considered and then submitted to the Ministry of Justice for approval.

County magistrate accused of bribery and torture: Chen Qun, a resident of Su County, telegraphed the High Court yesterday (2nd), stating that the resident was involved in a civil lawsuit in the county government. The county magistrate and the district chief colluded to solicit bribes from the resident, but were unsuccessful. They actually took the resident to the Chenghuang Temple in the middle of the night and used private torture to force a confession. Now he is only given one meal a day in prison. He requested relief. After receiving the petition, President Lin has sent someone to investigate thoroughly.

Fengxian

Continuing to build roads by conscripting labor: The Construction Bureau has received an order from the Department to continue building roads by conscripting labor. The County Political Conference discussed the measures and decided to first build the Fengzhe Road, that is, to use the Qin Gong Seawall from Fengcheng to Zhelin, which is more than 30 li long. The industry will open on January 15th. The Construction Bureau technicians Chen Gongzhao and others have been sent to investigate. However, in order to balance the labor throughout the county, the districts that have already conscripted labor in the previous session will be excluded, and only the first, fourth, and fifth districts that have not yet conscripted labor will be ordered to build.

Department to investigate the situation of the converted fields: The case of converting fields for grain transportation in our county has been repeatedly requested by local agencies to postpone the implementation. The Department ordered an investigation and is awaiting approval. It is now known that the Department has sent committee member Zhang Desheng to Fengxian on the 28th of last month to investigate the actual situation of the converted fields and to consult with party and government agencies in detail. At the same time, representatives of the tenant farmers Liao Wang and others went to pay their respects and requested that public opinion be adopted and the matter be handled slowly. Although no key points were obtained on the spot, committee member Zhang expressed before leaving that the situation of planting cotton in the converted fields in our county is indeed different from the situation of planting rice in the converted fields in Songjiang and Jinshan counties, and should be handled separately. He has already returned to the province yesterday to report.

Wuxi

Shocking news of a human head flying into the classroom: At about 3:00 pm the other day, a human head suddenly flew in from outside the wall into the classroom of the second grade of the primary school at the Hu Family Public School in Yanqiao Town, Fifth District (Tianshang City). The head was slightly black in color and had no neck. The teachers and students were all stunned by the sight, fearing that something would happen. They immediately dismissed school early and buried the head in the wilderness.

Rice boat robbed at Ya Cheng Bridge: Zhang Rongtai, a rice merchant from Changzhou, recently hired a boat and traveled to Wuxi to purchase rice in Yiyang. The other day, he arrived at Ya Cheng Bridge in our county in the evening and anchored the boat overnight. Unexpectedly, at about 2:00 am, a bandit boat suddenly came and six or seven bandits jumped out. They robbed the boat, tied up the boat owner Zhang Rongtai and the three crew members, and threatened them with pistols to keep silent. The boat owner resisted slightly and was severely beaten by a bandit with an iron ruler, injuring his leg. The bandits then wantonly searched and robbed for an hour before carrying the loot and jumping onto the bandit boat, speeding north. The rice boat was robbed of more than 300 yuan. Bandits rob in broad daylight and are arrested on the spot: Li Wang, a resident of Xinxiang, outside the North Gate of our county, went to Gaochangan the other day afternoon at about 1:00 pm for something. Unexpectedly, when she walked near the Zhangjia Stone Bridge, a bandit suddenly came from behind and stopped Li Wu and prevented her from going. He threatened her to keep silent and then searched her body. She was robbed of five yuan in banknotes, two yuan in current money, four jiao in silver coins, and dragged Li Wang to an abandoned tomb and beat her. Li Wang immediately shouted for help. At that time, the villagers nearby heard the sound and gathered to rescue her and captured a bandit and sent him to the Public Security Fifth Precinct. After the director of the precinct opened a trial, the bandit confessed that his name was Jiang Changgen, a native of Qingyang, Jiangyin, 32 years old. He directly admitted to robbing Li Wu of silver. Director Zhou prepared a document yesterday and sent him to the Public Security Bureau for interrogation.

Total strike in cotton mills throughout the county: The silk mills in Wuxi are suffering from a slump in the silk market and poor business. They originally planned to implement a shutdown, but in order to maintain the livelihood of the workers, they reluctantly started their cars. Later, labor-capital disputes suddenly occurred. The county government convened an arbitration meeting and decided to pay wages at a 10% discount. Unexpectedly, at about 1:00 pm the other day, a small number of troublemakers, starting from Zhou Shanbang, went to various silk mills to incite and force the female workers to strike. So, the 45 silk mills in Zhou Shanbang, Gongyun Bridge, and Ruichang, Qianfeng, Qian Shen, Qian Tai, San Tai, Yong Sheng, and other places outside the southeast gate successively stopped the cars. By about 5:00 pm, the silk mills throughout the county had fallen into a total strike. County Magistrate Shen has seriously investigated and dealt with the agitators. Yesterday morning, female workers from various silk mills gathered near the railway station. The Public Security Bureau and the Police Brigade sent police to suppress and maintain order. Suspect Wang Xiaomei and others were arrested and sent to the county for interrogation and bail. A propaganda team organized by five groups, including the party, government, police, labor, and silk mill trade unions, is now propagandizing and persuading people everywhere to resume work today. This can be called a troublesome labor tide.

Changzhou

The Township Head of Yulin Was Robbed Three Times

Wang Huo, the township head of Yulin Township, First District, Wuyi County, was robbed once on the 19th of last month, losing a self-defense box gun and an attempted abduction of his younger brother failed. On the night of the 26th, dozens of bandits came again and fired their guns as a warning, taking away two oxen used for plowing. On the night of the 27th, the bandits brought several civilian boats with weapons and carried away rice, wheat, clothing, and other supplies. Afterwards, they threatened to burn down his house and kill all his brothers. punish the bandits according to law.

Zhenjiang

Confirmation of Ma Yuren's Death

Ma Yuren, the bandit leader in Jiangbei, was previously ambushed by Chief Xiao Li of the Security Office at Baogang, under the jurisdiction of the Salt Office, and was shot three times. He was rescued by his bandit followers and escaped to Dalian for medical treatment. The Security Office received a confirmed telegram from Dalian yesterday stating that the bandit Ma Yuren died of his injuries at a hospital in Dalian on the date of Qiao of last month. The people of Jiangbei are now rid of this major scourge, and the general public can live and work in peace.

After repeated investigations by the county government, the case was deemed important. On the 2nd, Political Police Chief Wu Boyuan was specifically ordered to escort him to the Temporary Military Law Office for interrogation.

Bandits Openly Extort Money

On the evening of the 30th, more than a dozen bandits, each carrying weapons, broke into the house of Zhu Shineng, a wealthy household in Shuangpai Lake Dang Village, outside the east gate. Some bandits acted as lookouts while two bandits approached Zhu and negotiated in an unusually friendly manner. Several other bandits went to the nearby homes of Xu Shilin, Xu Laosan, and others, chatting and laughing as they went, then negotiating to borrow money, eventually demanding that the three families, including Zhu, pay 500 silver dollars within five days. Surprisingly, the bandits lingered all night, and did not leave until around 7:00 a.m. the next morning.

Nantong

A Rural Woman's Cleverness Backfires

Shi Fei, a rural woman from the Guanyin Mountain area of Tongyi, went to the County Court on the 2nd to sue Wang Nenghui for assault, accusing Wang of using a wooden pestle to directly strike her vaginal area, causing her to be injured and bedridden, requesting an examination. After Prosecutor Zhu's examination, it was determined that the bloodstains on her cotton pants and quilt were pig's blood, and there were no injuries to her lower body. The plaintiff was detained, causing a stir far and wide and becoming a laughingstock.

Preventing Sea Bandit Raids

Because the sea connects to Nantong, and the sea bandits Pan Kaiwu and Shen Guanxi joined forces after the fire, about seven or eight hundred of them infiltrated and harassed Lvsi Port. The county government has specifically dispatched police, together with water police patrol boats, to block and attack them.

Coastal Ports Implemented Blockades

Because the sea bandits around the Sanjia Town, Haimen, and Da'an Port areas of Nantong had already fled to the ocean after being suppressed by Shandong police, and because news has recently come that the pirate ships have run out of straw and planned to land and loot, all ports are implementing port closures to prevent the pirates from being resupplied, since winter fishing households are not released to the sea.

County District Chiefs Went to the Province to Await Questioning

The district chiefs of all eighteen districts of the county reported that Yan Nan, the county police captain, was corrupt and illegal. The provincial government will arrest Yan and bring him to military court for questioning. The complainants were notified to go to testify and all the district chiefs gathered in the city on the 2nd and will bring their documents to the province on the 4th to await questioning.

Yangzhou

Counterfeit Grain Certificates Escorted to the County for Interrogation

The Jiangdu Finance Bureau, due to the recent frequent discovery of counterfeit grain certificate cases, had ordered all counter clerks to pay attention to inspection. It was learned that yesterday (the 1st), a certificate for the grain payment of a certain Hua household was found to be counterfeit by the counter clerk at the county government treasury. After questioning, it was found that the old certificate from last year was given by the deceased and dismissed clerk Chen Tonggeng. The report was immediately made to the Finance Bureau, which summoned Chen to the bureau for questioning. He confessed without denial, and after repeated questioning by the counter clerks, Chen Tonggeng had no choice but to produce a list of counterfeit certificates. Director Tong has now escorted Chen to the county government for interrogation.

The Cause of a Young Woman's Death Is Unclear

In Dazhima Alley in this city, there is a man named Ding Yu. His wife, Chen, who was in her twenties, was initially betrothed by her parents to a shop assistant in a business shop. However, because the woman was unwilling, the engagement was dissolved. She then remarried to Ding for just over forty days. For some unknown reason, the woman suddenly committed suicide by poisoning herself the other day. The woman's father, Chen Xiaolin, believes that the cause of his daughter's death is unclear and plans to request a court inquest.

Xiaoshan

Sudden Collapse of Sandy Land in Eastern Township

In the past, the Qiantang sandy land often collapsed. In recent years, the authorities have paid attention, and fortunately, nothing has happened. Unexpectedly, on the 27th, 28th, and 29th, the sandy land in Shushan and Xushan in the eastern township of Xiaoshan was suddenly immersed in river water and collapsed for five or six li. The local residents were unable to escape in time and were swept away by the flood for the most part. Even those who escaped were left with nothing, carrying their children and lacking any means to recover. The aftermath was a scene of weeping and wailing, the situation was tragic.

Bengbu

The Bandit Gang Passing Through Woyang Has Been Defeated

Woyang in northern Anhui and Yongcheng in eastern Henan border each other and have always been areas where bandits emerge. At the end of last month, a large gang of bandits, mixed with the defeated soldiers of Sun Dianying's troops and about seven or eight hundred communists from Suxian County, infiltrated the territory from the junction of northwestern Woyang and Yongcheng, burning, killing, raping, and looting in the Mazhuka collection area, which was extremely fierce. Upon receiving the report, the three-county militia headquarters of Woyang, Mengcheng, and Hao County dispatched the Woyang militia to intercept them. They clashed with the bandits in the Hechang Town area for a day and night of fierce fighting. The bandits were unable to withstand the pressure and fled in disarray to the north. More than a hundred male and female hostages were rescued on the spot. Dozens of bandits were killed or wounded, and the militia soldiers were also killed or wounded around seven or eight. The 270th Regiment of the 45th Division, led by Liu Zi, arrived from Fuyang to reinforce the local defense, further strengthening the force. The militia is now searching for the remaining bandits and concurrently organizing the clearing of the countryside.

Educational News Highlights

Zhongshan Physical Education College Scout Troop Camps in Zhenjiang

Zhenjiang, 3rd: The scout training class of the Suzhou Zhongshan Physical Education College camped in Zhenjiang. On the first day, they invited Director Zhang of the Provincial Party Department's Training Department to review and welcome the scout instructors from the province. On the second day, they visited the Jiankang torpedo boats and toured various scenic spots. On the third day, they invited Professor Lu Jingsun to lecture on electricity, and returned to Suzhou in the afternoon.

Opening of the Waigang Public Education Center

The Waigang District Public Education Center in Jiading held its opening ceremony on November 30th, along with a supplementary oath ceremony. The Bureau of Education specially sent Supervisor Yang to supervise the oath ceremony and deliver a speech. Dr. Chuan Baochen, a representative from the Wuxi Education College, lectured on public education. In addition, students from the Waigang Central Elementary School performed arts, and the Kuishan Public Education Center performed a costumed speech. Approximately five or six hundred people participated.

General Meeting of the Zhabei Teachers' Union

The Joint Association of Municipal School Teachers and Staff of the Zhabei District of this city held its general meeting yesterday afternoon at the Municipal Feihong School. More than one hundred people from thirteen schools attended. The presidium consisted of Feng Xiwu, Zhou Darong, and Feng Chengxin. The records were kept by Zhang Xiaotian and Kong Yimin. The master of ceremonies was Zhang Xuelin. The speakers were Zhong, a representative from the Municipal Party Department, and Li Dachao, a representative from the Municipal Education Bureau. The meeting began at 2:00 p.m. with the usual ceremonies. First, Chairman Feng reported on the past work of the association. Then, Fang Zhenguan and Shen Baiying gave speeches. Mr. Fang's topic was the standardization and interspersion of phonetic symbols, and Mr. Shen's topic was a comparison of the old and new curriculums. After the speeches, the following motions were discussed: (1) A motion to establish a subject-based study group was passed and entrusted to the new executive committee. (2) A suggestion to the Education Bureau to request phased construction of the district's elementary schools was retained. (3) A motion on how to resolve the remaining funds of the Shanghai South-Zhabei Yangjing Teachers' Union was entrusted to the next executive committee. (4) A motion to determine the number of executive and supervisory committee members was passed, with eleven executive committee members, five alternates, three supervisory committee members, and two alternate supervisors. (5) A practical motion to collect membership fees was passed, with a fee of half a dollar per person per semester, to be collected after approval from the authorities. (6) A motion to publish regular publications was passed, with one issue per semester. (7) A motion on whether the association should create membership badges was rejected. After the motions were discussed, the executive committee members were elected. The elected members were Zhou Darong, Zhang Xiaotian, Kong Yimin, Lu Renjie, Yi Deben, Feng Xiwu, Ni Zhenrong, Zhang Xibei, Gao Tong, Zhu Yiming, and Xu Suying. The alternate members were Shi Zhengui, Zhu Xiaobei, and others. The supervisory committee members were Feng Chengxin, Jiang Manqian, and Zhou Zizhen. The alternate members were Zhang Fen and Yuan Zhicai. Finally, a representative from the Municipal Party Department gave guidance, and a group photo was taken before the meeting adjourned at a little over 6:00 p.m.

The Issue of the Validity Period for City-Certified Party Teachers

The Training Department of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department certified a class of primary and secondary school Party ideology teachers in the 17th year of the Republic, and their original validity period expired this autumn. The department had previously asked the Central Committee whether it could continue to be valid. It is now reported that an order has been issued approving its temporary validity. It is reported that the department has formally published a notice in the newspaper to inform everyone.

Jinan University Organizes a Book Committee２

Scouts Render Excellent Service

Jinan University is a place where talents gather. In addition to the stipulation that each college should publish periodicals of teachers' and students' research results separately to promote academics, the school will also organize a book committee to review and compile teachers' original works, systematic works, and translations of famous works from various countries, including the Forest Science Series. The school will fund the printing and provide bonuses to the authors to show encouragement. It is expected that the contribution to culture will not be limited to overseas Chinese alone. In addition, when the school's scout troop held an exhibition at the request of the local Shanghai Fine Arts School, they maintained order. One evening, the carpentry classroom was accidentally set on fire, and the scouts tried their best to put it out. At that time, the school's auditorium was holding a variety show with over a thousand spectators who were not alarmed. The principal thanked them repeatedly.

World Society Held a General Meeting Yesterday

Zhang Yifan Reports on Association Affairs

It Was Resolved That the General Assembly Would Move to Nanjing

The Shanghai World Society held its Shanghai member congress yesterday at the China Association. Gu Ziren, the standing committee member of the association, presided over the meeting and reported the purpose of the meeting. Then, Zhang Yifan, the executive secretary, introduced new members and reported on the association's affairs, saying that the association was initiated in Changsha in the 13th year of the Republic by Xu Qingyu, Chou Yishan, Yi Yincun, and others, with the purpose of studying world academics and communicating Eastern and Western cultures. In the spring of the 16th year, the initiators successively studied abroad and returned to Shanghai to reorganize and publish the Zhinao Weekly, edited by Xu Qingyu. They also published a series of books on the National Studies of Han Fei from the past 2,500 years. Gu Ziren went to the United States to give speeches. In the 17th year, they published books on American Philosophy Review in four lectures, Chinese Nationalities and World Culture, History of Curriculum Evolution in Chinese Schools, and Modern Political Thought. Shen Tilan went to India, Guo Luoanan, He Nan, and Xu Qingyu went to Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Guangdong, and other places to give academic lectures. Li Gong, a member sent to the United States to study by Limin, and Chen Weikun. In November, they moved from No. 20 Museum Road to the current location at No. 130 Yong'anli, North Sichuan Road. In the 18th year, Gu Ziren went to England to inspect academic affairs, and Li Youmin resigned, replaced by Shen Sizhuang and Zhang Renzhang. In July, they reorganized the World Monthly Magazine, which was later edited by Cao Liang. In the 19th year, they opened the World Society Bookstore and published books such as Marriage Revolution, The Exposure of Japan's Conspiracy Against China, and Collection of Academic Lectures on the Post-War American Economy. He Jiangheng came to serve as secretary. In August, they changed the publication plan and stopped publishing the World Monthly Magazine. Finally, they encouraged each other with continued efforts to study academics, communicate culture, and promote great unity. Then, the chairman delivered a speech, saying that Secretary Zhang had been loyal and diligent in his service over the years. Although the association's finances were not prosperous and he was paid a salary, it was still mostly voluntary. He had been misunderstood due to official affairs, but he had no complaints. He represented the members in expressing his gratitude. Then, Committee Member Shen Tilan gave an economic report, with a total income and expenditure of over 47,900 yuan. Next, the affairs of the association were discussed. As Nanjing was the academic center and had more members, it was resolved to move the General Assembly to Ning. The Shanghai Rongjian Branch was appointed with Zhang Yixun, Gu Ziren, and Li Gongpu as the committee members (Shen Tilan, Tan Bozhi, and Zeng Yuyu were inclined). They would meet with the members in Ning to study all matters. The meeting dispersed, and in the course of the meeting, Li Gongpu reported on his experiences of studying abroad and traveling in Europe to attend the International Peace Conference, which was both humorous and enjoyable.

The Guanghua Team Won the Jiangnan University Football Match Against Fudan

A Score of Two to One

| University Students Using Force in Football | Alas!

Yesterday, the Jiangnan University Sports Association's football championship between Fudan and Guanghua was replayed at Jiangwan. As a result of the fierce battle, Guanghua won with a score of two to one. The two sides actually staged a violence play. Most of the spectators were students from the two schools. Although Guanghua's journey was long, nine cars of people went to watch, and the motive for the fight originated from these nine cars of people. Although the level of university football has been improved in recent years, the bad habits of university students have not been changed. Every competition often involves violence, which is so crude and deplorable.

During the first half, Guanghua's Xi Qiaosheng scored a goal after receiving a pass from Yang Renwei. During the competition, a Fudan player fell on Guanghua's spectators by the sideline, and the Guanghua students punched him. Guanghua player Xi Qiaosheng also stepped forward to help beat the Fudan students. The cheering squad of Fudan students stepped forward to mediate, and the situation calmed down after three or two minutes, but from then on, fighting occurred during the game.

At the beginning of the second half, Fudan's momentum was extremely strong, and the ball was often in front of Guanghua's goal. Fudan had two opportunities to take a twelve-yard penalty, but unfortunately both were missed. Instead, Guanghua's Xi Qiaosheng scored another goal. Fudan tried to retaliate, and right winger Li Lin crossed the ball, and Yu Shunzhang headed it in, resulting in a score of two to one, with Guanghua winning. In the middle of the second half, referee He Chunhui saw that the players on both sides were in conflict, and Guanghua's Zhang Changjiang and Fudan's Yu Guzhang were wrestling and fighting. The referee immediately disqualified the two. Guanghua's Xi Qiaosheng was the main instigator of the violence, so he was closely guarded by many Fudan players in the second half and had very few opportunities to move around.

Table Tennis Federation Staff Meeting

International player Arima has nine contestants.

The Union will start registration today.

The Shanghai Table Tennis Federation held a staff meeting yesterday at the Jiande Association to discuss the Arima Earl Cup competition between China and Japan and to launch the Union Cup competition. Those who attended were Yu Binqi (Chairman), Lu Xiuli, Yang Jinqing, and Lu Zhongqiu, among others. The following resolutions were made: The China-Japan International Arima Earl Cup is scheduled to be held in mid-December. Nine players have been selected, including Lu Zhongqiu, Zhou Jianwen, Lu Xiuli, Lu Shentong, Luo Hongsheng, and Huang Xiangfa. The remaining three will be determined through challenges among top players. Registration for the Union Cup will begin today. The registration fee is one yuan per team per year and two yuan for competition. Each team can register nine to fifteen players. The International Table Tennis Rules will be adopted. The referees will be rotated by the team leaders and officers. The Federation will dispatch referees for important matches. The championship prize will be three silver shields, named after the characters "Union," "League," and "Association." It will be temporarily divided into three groups. The number of groups will depend on the number of teams that register. The Federation will review the technical skills of the registered teams and allocate them to the groups. A round-robin system will be implemented. The team with the most points in each group will win a championship, and a silver shield will be awarded. The teams that win championships will then compete in a round-robin final. The winner will receive a large silver cup and will retain it for one session. Teams that win three consecutive sessions or four sessions in total will retain it permanently. The registration locations are: Hu Qiankun at the Jiande Association office on Fusheng Road; Yu Binqi at the Chinese Typewriter Company on Nanjing Road, Jiangxi Road intersection; Lu Zhongqiu at the General Post Office. You can register nearby. Men and women are welcome to participate.

Local News

Taxpayers' Association Held General Meeting Yesterday

Resolution to Reject Water Rate Increase Proposal

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association held a general meeting at 4 PM yesterday to discuss the water rate increase proposed by the water company. More than 30 people attended, including Wang Xiaolai, Xu Ji, Yu Qiaqing, Hu Mengjia, Xu Xinliu, Liu Hongsheng, Zhang Zilian, Wu Yaiqin, Chu Fucheng, Sun Jingxi, Zhu Peiyuan, Yuan Jinchu, Cao Zhigong, Zhang Yichen, Shen Tianxin, Wen Lanting, Fang Jiaobo, Zhu Yinjiang, Lufei Bohong, Hu Qinxiang, Wu Yunzhai, Hu Xisheng, Lin Kanghou, Li Bohan, Pan Xulun, Yan Esheng, Wang Yansong (representing Yan Esheng), Jiang Yinan, Zhang Rulin, Chen Tianyin, Lu Fengzhu, Xie Zhongfu (representing Wu Yaiqin), Ye Fuxiao, and others. After Chairman Wang Xiaolai conducted the formalities, he first reported that the executive committee on the water rate increase issue had, in accordance with the resolution of the previous general meeting, appointed three committee members, Pan Xulun, Yu Xiji, and He Dekui, to audit the water company's accounts. The audit has now been completed, and the general meeting has been reconvened for discussion. Next, Representative He Dekui of the Audit Committee read the audit report (see the special column). Then, Secretary Tao Leqin reported the opinions of the Shanghai Real Estate Association (see yesterday's newspaper). Discussion then began, with Li Bohan, Hu Fengxiang, Zhang Zilian, Lin Kanghou, Shen Tianxin, Yuan Jinchu, Pan Xulun, Lufei Bohong, Yan Esheng, and others expressing their opinions one after another. After detailed discussion among the attendees, a unanimous resolution was passed to reject the water company's proposed increase in surcharges and modification of the contract. The reasons for their opposition were: (1) excessive interest guarantees and dividend distribution; (2) incomplete installation of water meters; (3) excessive expenses; (4) distribution of bonus shares; (5) bonus shares should not be guaranteed interest. The matter of alcohol should be handled by the executive committee.

Trade Associations Held Joint Meeting Yesterday to Discuss Trade Regulations

More than 200 Trade Associations Attended

Multiple Important Cases Resolved

The city's various trade associations held their second meeting of industry representatives yesterday to discuss industry regulations. More than 200 representatives from over 100 trade associations, including the dried goods industry, attended, including Ye Huijun, Zheng Chengqing, Sun Choucheng, Mao Chunpu, Yuan Mingjun, and Lu Fengzhu. Chairman Zheng Chengqing, Ye Jiaxing, Sun Choucheng, and Mao Chunpu conducted the formalities. Chairman Zheng Chengqing then reported on the efforts to petition in Beijing. The report is as follows:

Report: Everyone, it has been more than a month since the previous meeting entrusted us with handling the issue of trade regulations. In truth, our achievements have been minimal. However, we have never forgotten the mission entrusted to us by the last meeting, but our strength is limited, so please forgive us. The importance of trade regulations, as past facts and experiences tell us, lies in the fact that under the old guild system, if an apprentice could not obtain a guild certificate after completing his apprenticeship, he could not be employed by the same industry. If a member of the same industry could not obtain a guild certificate, he could not operate. Therefore, industries with guild organizations made daily progress in their skills, and the unity of the guilds was very strong. Since the reorganization of guilds into trade associations, those with trade regulations have been able to maintain their original unity, while those without trade regulations have experienced undesirable situations such as encroachment, seizure of business, and disruption of public affairs. Those engaged in international trade have lost international credibility and reduced export business. Those who set up shops to engage in retail business have damaged the credibility of the entire industry and harmed society. Just look at the facts in recent years. For example, the intestine industry, which specializes in sales to European and American countries, originally had an excellent position in international trade. A portion of the livelihoods of the agricultural and commercial sectors depended on it. However, because those in this industry lacked a trade association organization, they raised prices to buy and sold at low prices, and secretly mixed inferior goods. As a result, business could not be sustained, and after being shipped abroad for inspection, they were deemed a health hazard and even banned from import. In recent years, the intestine industry's trade association has worked hard to gradually restore its former glory. Another example is the mahjong tile industry. A few years ago, sales abroad were extremely prosperous. However, due to mutual encroachment among those in this industry, and the lack of trade regulations to restrict them, they reduced labor and stole materials. As a result, the governments of various countries took measures to restrict imports. These are all major losses in international trade, and everyone knows it. Even more widespread are situations such as mutual disruption, destruction, damage to credibility, and harm to society. Therefore, when the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce held its first meeting of member representatives to discuss this issue, all industries expressed sympathy. Subsequently, a request was submitted to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for approval. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce, which oversees commerce nationwide, also knows that trade regulations are essential for maintaining the commercial sector and improving the trade association. It must be able to give us a satisfactory response. Who knew that the responsible personnel of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce did not understand commercial conditions and were rejected? This was truly unexpected. Afterwards, they persisted in their prejudices and did not think about rescuing the situation, claiming that trade regulations had no legal basis in the laws. However, upon checking Article 2 of the Trade Association Law, the purpose of a trade association is to increase and maintain public interest and correct business abuses. Trade regulations are one way to achieve this purpose. This has a strong basis in this law. Furthermore, upon checking Article 1 of the Civil Law on Debt, in the absence of law, custom and trade regulations are the written customs of an industry. This also has a very definite legal status. We see the above facts and laws. This time, the united request of various industries to approve trade regulations is truly a work that is needed based on actual needs and within the scope permitted by law. From the last meeting of industry representatives to now, it has been more than a month. During this month, the work that has been done is that all industries and unions have jointly appealed. At the National Industry and Commerce Conference, thanks to the efforts of Mr. Wang Yansong and Bureau Director Wang Xiaoyan, Jiaobo, Ye Huijun and other gentlemen, it was finally passed at the National Industry and Commerce Conference and sent to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for adoption and implementation. To urge the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to implement it as soon as possible, the Committee for the Protection of Trade Regulations sent representatives to Beijing on the 18th of last month to petition the National Government and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, who have paid considerable attention to it. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce will also hold a departmental meeting to discuss this matter, which shows that it has attracted attention. Chambers of commerce in places such as Dongtai, Hangzhou, and Liaoning in Zhejiang have all unanimously expressed their support, which has aroused a nationwide trend. However, those who travel a hundred miles are halfway through at ninety. How to proceed from here depends on the unanimous efforts of various industries to decide on a strong plan so that various industries can follow this decision gradually to achieve good results. Therefore, we are convening the second meeting of industry representatives today to discuss the future plan of action, hoping that the representatives present will express their opinions and decide on the steps we should take. At the same time, for the sake of our own interests, we should request the National Government and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to dismiss and punish the responsible personnel who do not understand commercial conditions and make rash rejections of trade regulation issues. Next, Representative Ye Huijun of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce delivered a speech, stating that trade regulations are a major track for the development of commerce. If the industry can disregard the regulations, it is like losing the track, and the commercial sector will inevitably be chaotic. Therefore, the issue of trade regulations is truly a matter of life and death for our country. Brothers recently met with Chairman Chiang and Mayor Zhang and stated that there should be a satisfactory reply.

Discussion: (1) The Guangdong Dry Goods Industry proposed that trade associations in all industries should, in the spirit of mutual assistance, sanction non-member industries and industry members who disrupt trade regulations. The resolution was to retain it. (2) The Intestine Industry, Dried Goods Industry, and New Drug Industry jointly sent a telegram to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce urging them to implement it as soon as possible, stating that all industries that have not yet joined must abide by the trade regulations. The resolution was to pass it. (3) A telegram was sent to the National Government to order the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to implement the resolution as soon as possible. The resolution was to pass it. (4) Before the trade regulations formulated by the trade association have been ordered by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce to be universally observed by all industries that have not yet joined, the acceptance of matters entrusted by government agencies will be temporarily suspended. The resolution was to pass it. In a temporary motion, it was proposed that the General Assembly send a telegram in its name to Mayor Zhang to forward it to Chairman Chiang, requesting that measures be taken to maintain order. The resolution was passed. The original telegram reads: Nanjing Central Hotel telegraphic message to Shanghai Mayor Zhang Yuejun Jian: Today, the various industries held a meeting of representatives. The group was excited about the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's rejection of the trade regulation case. Please forward it to Chairman Chiang to seek a solution to maintain commercial conditions. Shanghai Municipal Trade Association Representatives General Assembly bows.

Issue of Sino-Foreign Joint Venture Stores Joining the Chamber of Commerce

Should be limited to registration with Chinese officials in accordance with the law. The Municipal Chamber of Commerce believes that Sino-foreign joint venture companies and stores should be limited to registration with Chinese officials in accordance with the law to join the Chamber of Commerce or trade associations as members. It has submitted a request to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for supplementary explanation and sent a letter to the Silk Factory Trade Association for reference. The original text is as follows:

Submission to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce, Nanjing: Inquiries about whether Sino-foreign joint venture companies and stores in the city's copper, iron, and machine industries can join trade associations should be forwarded by the affiliated associations for review. The case has been submitted to the Central Government for approval and forwarded for instructions. However, upon checking the additional restrictions, there are considerable restrictions on the amount of capital, voting rights, and number of company directors, but the fact that the company or store must first register with Chinese officials is not listed as one of the conditions. It is naturally because Article 11 of the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law already has regulations that there is no need to repeat them. However, upon checking Article 16 of the Implementing Rules of the Trade Association, all regulations that apply to the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law are listed. However, Article 11 of the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law is not included among those listed. If a Sino-foreign joint venture store requests to join a trade association, although its capital, voting rights, and number of directors meet the regulations of the Ministry, it has not registered with Chinese officials. The trade association has no laws and regulations to rely on to reject it in accordance with laws and regulations. If it wants to reluctantly accommodate it, it is afraid that various disputes will arise due to registration jurisdiction issues. How should it be handled? Should there be supplementary regulations to deal with it? I hereby submit this telegram to your department for review, hoping that you will give instructions for compliance. It will be convenient for everyone. Shanghai Chamber of Commerce bows.

Letter to Silk Factory Industry: Dear Sir/Madam, On the 2nd of this month, we received a letter stating that some Sino-foreign joint venture companies and stores are registered with the British government in Hong Kong or with the US government in the State of Delaware. Once legal relations arise, they are not subject to the sanctions of Chinese law. Therefore, the Chamber of Commerce allowing these companies and stores to be members is tantamount to admitting foreign merchants as members. Please provide an explanation to dispel doubts. Upon investigation, Article 11 of the Implementing Rules of the Chamber of Commerce Law states that store members should have a store within this area and have been registered in accordance with the law. Therefore, Sino-foreign joint venture companies and stores must first register with Chinese officials in accordance with the law and obtain the legal status of a Chinese business before they can join the association. The so-called companies and stores registered in the UK and the US cannot obtain membership status in accordance with the law. The worry that they will not be subject to Chinese law is naturally not a problem. I hereby send a letter to inform you. Sincerely, Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association

How to Commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising?

The few cannons fired by the Zhaohe warship indirectly caused Yuan Shikai's death. The campaign to overthrow Yuan Shikai was a joint effort by many revolutionary forces within the country to fight against a traitorous and extremely cunning figure. They finally managed to defeat him. However, Yuan Shikai's ghost is still rampant throughout the country. Moreover, through his years of manipulating power, he caused the entire nation to lose its sense of integrity and shame, and the country's vitality was almost completely depleted. The remnants of the imperial system have not been completely eliminated to this day. The traitor Yan Xishan is a clear example. At the time when Yuan Shikai declared himself emperor, Yan Xishan was the first to urge him to do so, greatly appreciated by Yuan Shikai, who even granted him the title of first-class marquis. This kind of shameless warlord should have long been despised by the people of the country. Yet, he still raises troops to initiate unrest and undermine unification. All of these are the toxic legacy of Yuan Shikai. Therefore, commemorating the Zhaohe Uprising should involve thoroughly eradicating all remnants of feudalism.

Furthermore, the target that the Zhaohe Uprising aimed to eliminate was Yuan Shikai. Yuan Shikai's self-proclaimed imperial system was subjectively due to his disregard for the people of the country and his excessive ambition. But objectively, it was due to the fact that many people at the time held illusions of being ruled and living in peace, and did not engage in building a stable and secure society. Moreover, members of the successful party abandoned their original aspirations, even disregarding the principles of the revolution, thinking that the Prime Minister's ideals were too lofty. This led the Prime Minister to sadly say, "I resigned from the presidency not because I feared the forces, but because I could not carry out the construction of the revolution." When we commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising, we should recognize that the chaos of warlord cycles in the decade or so after the founding of the Republic of China was entirely due to the failure to firmly believe in the Prime Minister's principles and policies, and the failure to follow the Prime Minister's revolutionary strategies, which inevitably led to this result. The Prime Minister's profound and comprehensive teachings are truly the only way to save and build the country, and it is an indispensable undertaking that cannot be ignored.

From this, it can be known that the Three Principles of the People of our party are the only effective solution for revolutionary nation-building. Before the Republic of China, our party and its principles were used to create the Republic of China. After the Republic of China, our party and its principles are used to defend and build the Republic of China. Anyone who intends to undermine the Republic of China, like Yuan Shikai and his ilk, is a public enemy of our party. In the end, they will inevitably fail. In recent years, rebellions by Long and others have frequently occurred, causing the construction projects to be delayed. Whether the implementation of political tutelage can proceed smoothly in the future, and whether the Prime Minister's wishes can be realized in the shortest possible time, all depend on whether the feudal remnants who disrupt the Republic of China and undermine peaceful unification can have their roots severed in the shortest possible period. All comrades and compatriots across the country should, when commemorating the Zhaohe Uprising today, unanimously recognize the difficult situation of the country, appreciate the arduous environment of the revolution, and further recognize that the victory of this campaign against the rebels is truly a victory for the Three Principles of the People. Support the spirit and enthusiasm of the martyrs in protecting the Republic of China, support the fundamental eradication of reactionaries by the party and government, and ensure that the ghosts and lingering aura of Yuan Shikai no longer haunt the territory of the Republic of China, so that the country can truly be unified and have lasting peace.

Slogans: (1) The Zhaohe Uprising was a courageous struggle against the imperial system and in defense of the Republic of China. (2) The Zhaohe Uprising was a manifestation of the patriotic spirit of the martyrs of our party. (3) The Zhaohe Uprising inherited the spirit of the Xinhai Revolution. (4) The Zhaohe Uprising was the precursor to the Yunnan Uprising. (5) The Zhaohe Uprising was a struggle between democratic forces and the remnants of autocracy. (6) The martyrs who died for the Zhaohe Uprising were the protectors of the Republic of China. (7) Promote the spirit of the Zhaohe Uprising, safeguard the Republic of China, and eliminate feudal reactionary forces. (8) Commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising to consolidate the foundation of the party and the country and promote the construction of political tutelage. (9) Commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising to severely punish Yan and Feng, the traitors who undermined unification and betrayed the central government. (10) Commemorate the Zhaohe Uprising to ensure lasting peace and promote the glory of China.
