The Nanyang Inspection Team Reports on Recent Conditions

Expressing the Pain of Unequal Customs Duties

The Nanyang Islands National Products Inspection Team, organized by the Shanghai National Products Factory Association, has already departed south. Yesterday, the association received a report from Mr. He Zijing and Mr. Lu Yifei, staff members of the Scientific Instrument Museum, from Singapore. They described the welcome received by local overseas Chinese in Saigon and the inspection of industry and commerce. They particularly lamented the oppression of imperialist tariffs on overseas Chinese. The following is a summary of their report: French Indochina, formerly known as Vietnam, was originally a tributary state of our country. Its territory is divided into three regions: Cochinchina, Annam, and Tonkin. Haiphong in Tonkin is an important gateway to Yunnan. Saigon and Cholon in Cochinchina are important cities in terms of politics and commerce. Annam produces abundant rice, and Saigon is the main export market. There is a train from Saigon to Haiphong and a long-distance bus to Siam, both of which can be reached in one or two hours. It is heartbreaking to see such a beautiful land fall into the hands of foreigners. The currency system of Annam is decimal. One Annam piastre is equivalent to about two Shanghai taels. After the establishment of the National Government, our country abolished the Sino-French Commercial Treaty. For a time, a new treaty was not concluded, and Chinese goods imported into France were taxed according to the example of countries without treaties. Since last year, the tax rate has been increased repeatedly. Any ordinary daily necessities are taxed at 100%, and the valuation is arbitrarily increased or decreased without any basis. Or, taxes are levied by weight, with 96 Annam piastres levied for every 100 kilograms (one kilogram is equivalent to 165 Chinese pounds). For example, a common, plain enamel basin, which costs only 50 or 60 cents in Shanghai, costs 2.5 piastres (equivalent to more than 3 Shanghai dollars) in Saigon, an increase of about six times. However, overseas Chinese are still enthusiastic about adopting them. If the tax issue is resolved, it will be quite beneficial to promote national products. The Sino-French New Treaty was signed last year, but it has not yet been implemented. The team will send a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Industry and Commerce after arriving in Singapore, and report to the association to work together to promote the implementation of the Sino-French New Treaty. Currently, the population of Cholon is 700,000, and overseas Chinese account for two-sevenths. Most of the industry and commerce are concentrated here. The group leader, Mr. Zhou Guojun's Nanfeng Company, is located there. Mr. Zhou is young and insightful and is relied upon by our country. The store clerks of Nanfeng are particularly helpful in guiding and directing. The Cholon Cochinchina Chinese General Chamber of Commerce held a tea reception at its hall at 3:00 pm on November 6. The president, vice-president, directors, and more than 30 well-known overseas Chinese businessmen attended. They discussed various ways to promote national products. There is a product showroom behind the chamber's hall, but unfortunately, there are not many items on display and they are very ordinary. The team plans to collect samples from various national product factories after returning to Shanghai and transport them for display to serve as an observation. If our manufacturers can broaden their horizons and make every effort to promote sales overseas, Nanyang will be a very good commercial outlet for our country.

Shanghai Bank Shareholders' Meeting

Increase Capital by 2.5 Million Yuan

Shanghai Commercial Savings Bank in this city, due to the daily expansion of its business and the increasing number of branches, the board of directors held two special meetings and resolved to increase its capital by 2.5 million yuan. At 2 pm on the 30th of last month, a special meeting of shareholders was convened at the Bankers' Association to discuss the issue of increasing capital. At that time, a total of 19,900 shares arrived, which was sufficient for the statutory three-quarters or more of the number of shares. The chairman of the bank's board of directors rang the bell to open the meeting. The chairman respectfully read the will and then announced the purpose of the meeting and the origin of the increase in capital. The general manager then reported on the business situation of the capital from small to large and the branches from few to many in the past fifteen years, as well as the reasons for increasing shares. Then, the chairman asked everyone to stand up and vote (the whole body stood up and passed). It is calculated that the original capital of the bank was 2.5 million yuan and the public reserve was 1.51 million yuan. Now, another 2.5 million yuan has been added to the shares, making a total of 5 million yuan. The public reserve has increased by 990,000 yuan, making a total of 2.5 million yuan. The bank has always taken serving the society, assisting industry and commerce, and developing international trade as its purpose. The branches have been established in 29 major cities in the country, and the business is progressing day by day. It is thought that after this share increase, the business of the head office and branches will be more developed.

Red Cross Receives Disaster Report from Yu County

The Chinese Red Cross Society yesterday received a telegram from various agencies and groups from the Yu County Party Committee and Yu County Government Relief Branch in Henan, reporting that the disaster situation obtained by the Henan Relief Association's investigation was heartbreaking and unbearable to witness. It is urgently disclosed as follows: (omitted) This time, Yan and Feng rebelled, and the overall situation of Yu County's disaster was telegraphed on the 7th of last month, requesting a glimpse. Now, the information obtained from the survey by the River Surface Relief Association will be stated one by one. (1) Population: 1,326 deaths and injuries. (2) Houses burned down: 4,085 rooms, calculated at 20 yuan per room, totaling 81,700 yuan. (3) Felled trees: 20 million trees, calculated at an average of 2 yuan per tree, totaling 400,000 yuan. (4) Forcibly requisitioned hundreds of thousands of civilians, requiring a total of 2.2 million yuan in expenses. (5) Military appropriations: 12 times, totaling 431,808.9 yuan. (6) Requisitioned grain: 14,834,750 catties, totaling 600,8814 yuan. (7) Searched for forage grass: 39,751,717 catties of grass, totaling 293,969 yuan, and 10,945,081 catties of feed, totaling 320,272 yuan. (8) Forcibly conscripted 1,800 soldiers, for a total loss of 180,000 yuan. (9) Forts occupied more than ten hectares of land, estimated at about 6 yuan per mu, totaling more than 6,000 yuan. (10) Loss of property: totaling 2,391,750 yuan. (11) Loss of livestock and vehicles: a total of 19,011 livestock, totaling 953,050 yuan, 5,081 large vehicles, totaling 203,240 yuan, and 2,335 small vehicles, totaling 9,340 yuan. According to statistics, the total loss is 7,849,943 yuan. As for the reduced harvest of the wheat and autumn crops due to the war, the death toll, or the escape of those who have not returned, is not included. It is estimated that the minimum loss in Yu County is more than 10 million yuan. Yu County has a population of 400,000, and each person averages about 30 yuan. The county has a total land area of more than 16,000 hectares. After deducting village bases, roads, sandy roads, and river banks, each person estimates that one mu of land yields a net profit of only about 3 yuan per month. With an income of 3 yuan, it bears a loss of more than 30 yuan, which is far apart. I have waited to reply according to the situation. The tax rate in Yu County is higher than that in the whole province. The historical records have been heavily taxed for 500 years, and the people are poor. In the "Records of Profits and Diseases of the Prefecture and Kingdoms", the county records, and the writings of township elites, the figures are difficult to enumerate. Since the Republic of China, internal wars have been frequent, and there have been requisitions every year. The father is heavier than other counties. In the autumn of the 16th year, there were more than three months of troops stationed on the border of the country, and the losses of supply and incineration in the northeast of the county were also more than 3 million yuan. The vitality was greatly damaged and has not yet recovered. This year's battle is following, and the suffering of searching outside of time is even unprecedented. In this case, after the destruction, it is said that if the levy is not suspended for ten years and a large amount of urgent relief is not issued, it will not be enough to benefit the disaster victims and appease the people. To this day, scholars have stopped studying, farmers sigh in the fields, and merchants have lost their jobs in the markets. The wounds have not yet healed and the escapes have not yet recovered. In addition to telegraphing the central government for special handling, I dare to cry and state the previous situation and implore you to observe the odd disasters and the heavy war disasters, and unanimously appeal to the central government to handle special cases, and to also relieve and assist the orphans or raise huge amounts of money to benefit the orphans. I urgently await orders. The Yu County Party Committee, the County Government Relief Branch, and various agencies and groups of the Kuomintang of China in Yu County, Henan kowtow.

The places where relief funds have not been paid are the Shaanxi Wugong Congee Factory, the Jiangsu Yancheng Winter Relief, the urgent relief in Taizhou, Zhejiang, and the Liaoning Beiping Congee Factory. The society's economy is so tight, and the urgent telegrams from Henan and Shaanxi provinces are flying like snowflakes, which is really against the will. Then, Chairman Wang said that the society's relief is based on conscience and has long been understood by all sectors. In this freezing weather, we can still have warmth and satiety. When we close our eyes and think about the suffering of the victims, how can we not be injured when we have no food when we are hungry and no front when we are cold? All gentlemen, please work hard to carry out the relief. There is no shortage of charitable comrades in Shanghai who will be able to promote the spirit of compatriotism and generously provide relief to the disaster victims. Zhang Weiyuan reported on the assistance to the disaster victims who were left behind in the Yifu Guxi Hua County of Henan, and they will be able to take the Ruiyang Maru to Wuhan tonight. Feng Yangshan reported that he had gone to Ninghai to inspect the reconstruction of the Zhongdu Bridge, and invited officials and gentry from Ninghai Tiantai to discuss changing the bridge body to be lower in order to make it permanent, and to draft several articles of association for the bridge construction office, which were approved. Local News II

Overseas Student Jin Chongling Drowned Himself

The deceased's belongings arrived in Shanghai yesterday.

Notice to Family Members to Collect and Authenticate

Whether there is a last will is still unknown.

The incident of Jin Chongling, a student studying in Japan, committing suicide by drowning himself has been kept very secret by the Japanese, resulting in very little knowledge of it in society. Now, because the belongings left by the student after his suicide have arrived in Shanghai, the shipping company has notified his family members to come to Shanghai. The following is a brief record of the matter for the reader's information, not to be viewed lightly.

Account of the Drowning Jin Chongling, a student studying in Japan, came from Nanjing to Shanghai to take a ship to Japan. Jin was not very financially well-off, so after arriving in Shanghai, he chose a ship with a cheaper ticket to cross the sea. The ship Jin took was the Sansaka Maru, a third-class cargo ship of the Japanese Post Office in this city, bound for Kobe. This ship had cheaper passenger tickets than the Shanghai Maru and other ships. After Jin boarded the ship, there was initially nothing unusual. However, when the ship reached the Yellow Sea, in the dead of night, amidst the sound of the turbulent waves, he sneaked out of the third-class cabin and climbed onto the deck and jumped into the sea. At that time, the ship was traveling very fast, so very few people knew about it.

The Body Was Not Recovered Passengers in the third-class cabin all live in the same cabin. After Jin Chongling drowned himself, some of his cabinmates noticed that he had left the cabin and had not returned. Suspecting something, they reported it to the crew members. After detailed investigation, the person was nowhere to be found. They searched the room and found a suicide note, but it did not mention the reason. At this time, it was late at night and the sea was wide and the sky was vast, and there was no way to recover the body. They had to leave it alone and only report it to the head office after arriving in Japan.

Baggage Sent to Taiwan by Mistake When the Sansaka Maru arrived in Japan, the shipowner collected his belongings and items in one place and immediately ordered them to be transferred to the Japanese Post Office ship returning to Shanghai so as to notify his family to come and claim them. Unexpectedly, in a hurry, Jin's luggage was mistakenly delivered to the Asahi Maru and taken to Keelung, Taiwan by the Asahi Maru. After discovering the mistake, it had already traveled thousands of nautical miles. It was brought back to Japan and then transferred to Shanghai again.

Notice to Jin's Family This trip was originally brought back to Kobe by the Asahi Maru, and then transferred to a Shanghai-bound ship. It was not brought to Shanghai until yesterday. The Japanese Post Office found that his family was in Nanjing, so it temporarily stored his luggage at the Shanghai warehouse and sent a letter from the agency to inform his family, Jin Shaowei reported that Jin Chongling had committed suicide by drowning and the reason was unknown. Whether there is a suicide note in the luggage, wait for the family to arrive at Shanghai Yangshupu No. 31, the warehouse, to claim it and then open it by themselves to clarify the truth. It also stated that the reason why the luggage was delayed and the notification was delayed was due to the mistaken delivery to the Taiwanese post ship. This letter will be sent by express delivery this morning. After his family arrives in Shanghai to open the luggage, the reason for Jin Chongling's suicide by drowning may be known.

Fan Yichun of Qibao Town Goes Missing

Four people came on bicycles

They dragged Fan away on the way

No news for two days

Fan Yichun, the owner of Fan Yongjihao, a shop in Qibao Town, Shanghai, is 28 years old. He has a wife and children and is of modest wealth, known as a petty bourgeois. He is particularly timid and does not have many friends. At around 2 PM on the first day of this month, Fan went out alone to visit the Zhang family, his wife's family, in Changbang. After an hour, Fan said goodbye and returned. On the way, he passed Guanyintang (a necessary road for going back and forth, near Qibao). He stopped at a friend's house and sat for a while before leaving for home. Unexpectedly, he had not walked a few steps when four people on bicycles sped up from behind and stopped Fan on the road. Without a word, they dragged Fan Yichun away. Afterwards, his family waited until late at night but did not see Fan return, and were greatly alarmed because Fan never stayed out overnight. The next morning, his family sent out scouts to inquire along the way. When they reached Guanyintang, they learned from the villagers who witnessed the incident that at around 3 PM on the first day, Fan was suddenly dragged away by four people on bicycles and disappeared without a word. The four people had been wandering around this area for several days. Furthermore, they repeatedly inquired and only said that the four people were from a certain organization. Then his family visited again and again to find out where they were, but there was still no whereabouts after two days. Therefore, his family is extremely anxious.

Old Dalai Returns to the United States This Morning

Opening Sino-American Air-Sea Combined Flights

Mr. Labour White Dalai, the owner of Dalai Foreign Firm, came to China this time to investigate the development of Far East trade and the Oriental shipping industry. He had contacted important figures of the National Government in the capital. Yesterday, because his work was completed, he took the Tatuo ship of his firm back to the United States. The expansion of business and the situation of returning to the country and leaving Shanghai are recorded as follows:

New Ships Sailing Sino-American Competition in the Pacific navigation industry is the fiercest this year. Each firm is building high-speed ships to sail. Mr. Dalai is also using 30 million US dollars to build two new 26,000-ton postal ships with a speed of 23 knots each, and according to the new method of the Atlantic Ocean, each of the two ships is equipped with two seaplanes for picking up and sending passengers and mail. For example, if the ship has arrived in Japan, Shanghai passengers can still be sent by plane, or those who have important matters that need to arrive at the destination first can also be changed from ship to plane. This kind of air-sea combined flight is the first in the Far East. One of the two ships has been launched and the other will be launched next month. In about six months, the route from San Francisco to Shanghai can be added. This is to arrange the procedures for the new ship's sailing schedule in advance.

Building a Radio Station The firm's business in China is huge, and the number of ships coming and going is increasing day by day. There are so many telegrams for its own use that it has decided to establish a radio station in Shanghai. However, in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Communications, it is limited to the firm's own ships. The materials have been shipped to Shanghai in batches and the radio station will be built immediately. Mr. Dalai's visit to Beijing this time was to contact the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications to discuss this matter. It is heard that there has been a result.

Staff Arrived in Port to See Off After the Shanghai Groups Held a Public Banquet Yesterday, Mr. Dalai went to the company on Guangdong Road in the morning and talked with the Chinese director Wu Hongyuan and Chuan Shengyuan for an hour. He discussed and planned a lot on business, and then ordered the company's Taft ship to set sail one day earlier this morning because he had to rush to San Francisco for Christmas. All the staff of the Shanghai company went to the port to see him off on the ship.

Leaving Shanghai for the United States This Morning Mr. Dalai, his wife and secretary took a small steamboat from the Xinguang Wharf to Yangshupu Hetong last night and transferred to the Taft big ship. Shanghai foreman Steve accompanied Mr. Dalai to Kobe, Japan, and then returned to Shanghai. Mr. Dalai went directly across the Pacific Ocean back to San Francisco. The ship left port at 7 am this morning.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Responds to the Batavia General Chamber of Commerce Letter Regarding the Xiao Case

Definitely not to expand on the basis of the situation

Actually seeking equal treatment

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce explained the true meaning of the anti-Dutch movement in the Xiao case and yesterday replied to the Batavia Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in a letter saying that it received a large letter from Zhan on the 2nd of this month saying that the Xiao case was only an indecent act by the crew of the Java Company. China and the Netherlands have always been friendly and it seems that it should not be over-expanded to affect the whole body. The various sectors requested the council to telegraph the information on their behalf. A copy of the original telegram is attached, hoping to forward it to all sectors and asking for a reply, etc. Under the rule of the countries where they are stationed, the opinions and actions of overseas Chinese in the Dutch colonies are severely restricted. This time, the overseas Chinese merchants strongly requested that the Xiao case should not be expanded too much, and there are difficulties of their own. The Chamber of Commerce and the merchants under its jurisdiction also deeply understand the difficulties of the position of the Chamber. However, considering that the taxation and other treatments of overseas Chinese compatriots who do business and reside in the Dutch colonies in Nanyang cannot be equal to those of Europeans and Japanese, but instead are reduced to being with the natives, the descriptions in newspapers and magazines and the spread of those who returned to the country for investigation are all true and reliable. Anyone with a bit of blood will be indignant and heartbroken. Because of the weakness of the national power, there is no way to clean up the situation and regret is used as a sigh. The layer of friendship between China and the Netherlands quoted in the letter seems not to be entirely true. The relationship between countries and the friendship between individuals are the same, and it can only be said to be true friendship if equal treatment can actually be achieved. This time, the humiliation of Ms. Xiao is a microcosm of the Dutch's long-standing contempt for the Chinese nation. The domestic public opinion in this case is to seek the cause of the fruit. On the one hand, we should try our best to punish the murderers and apologize to Ms. Xiao in order to stretch the law slightly. On the other hand, we should take this opportunity to try our best to seek equal treatment for the Chinese nation and overseas Chinese in the Netherlands, so that those who come to the south will not repeat the same mistakes, and the position of the overseas Chinese merchants in the Netherlands can be invisibly increased in the future and will no longer be treated like the natives of the past. All of these are considerations for the overall interests of the overseas Chinese compatriots in the Netherlands and are definitely not intentionally aggressive and want to use the Xiao case as a sign. This situation is that overseas Chinese compatriots are far away from the motherland, and it is not easy for domestic newspapers to popularize in Nanyang, so there is a lack of close understanding. It is inevitable that they will mistakenly think that the domestic boycott of Dutch ships is a show of expansion. Dare to briefly state the general situation and attach a copy of the minutes of the meeting of the various sectors of the country to support Xiao and the anti-Dutch support association and reply in a letter. I hope that you will check it. Sincerely, the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce in Batavia.

To re-state the grievances and plead for prompt prosecution according to law, Da Xun et al.'s lawsuit against Wu Desheng et al. of the Fuchang Military Uniform Factory was heard by Junchu on the 26th and 27th of last month, and Junchu orally ordered to file a public prosecution to the same-level trial court according to law on the same day. It is obvious that justice is there and will never allow cunning people to be at large outside the law, and Junchu's national legislative spirit is to rescue the suffering and punish the evil and punish the evil, making the three generations of justice return to today. The disease and cold are intertwined, and their lives are uncertain. It is not necessary to say more. For this reason, in addition to A Jin Xiao Sheng et al. quietly waiting for the summons, a certain number must reiterate the grievances and plead for Junchu to show mercy and file a lawsuit according to law as soon as possible, so that they can be tried as soon as possible, sentenced as soon as possible, relieved from litigation as soon as possible, and obtain fair relief as soon as possible. Please, the undersigned, Peng Daxun, Hao Shouzhi, et al.'s private prosecution agent lawyer Yan Lunkui, December 3, 19th year of the Republic of China.

Two-Road Police Investigation Bureau Cracked Many Theft Cases

Qiu Dingbao Requests Analysis of Inheritance Case Appeal

Judge advises reconciliation

Limited time to consider five days

Qiu Dingbao, the niece of the late paint tycoon Qiu Weiqing, requested that her brother Qiu Shensan divide the inheritance of her deceased father, but failed to do so. She then filed a lawsuit. The first instance judgment ordered Shensan to divide 10,000 yuan. Dingbao believed that her father's inheritance was 3 million, and even if it was as her brother said, it would be a million, but only getting 10,000 yuan was hard to convince her. Therefore, she filed an appeal. Then, for some unknown reason, she suddenly applied to withdraw the appeal. However, Shensan was still unwilling to sacrifice 10,000 yuan and also filed an appeal, causing Dingbao to re-file a collateral appeal, which was quite suspicious. Later, the High Court repeatedly opened the court, but Shensan never arrived. The presiding judge did not want the case to be suspended and issued a summons recently stating that if he refused to appear again, he would be detained and a hearing was scheduled for yesterday afternoon. Shensan, upon learning that he could not avoid it, but did not want to confront his sister in court, submitted a request to withdraw the appeal in advance. The High Court held that Dingbao had already filed a collateral appeal, so the court was still opened as scheduled. Judge Hu asked whether your brother had withdrawn the appeal, and what was your claim? Dingbao immediately said that even if her brother withdrew, she would have to proceed. Judge Hu then advised that she should value the relationship between siblings, that money was an external thing. If you withdraw the appeal now, you can get the 10,000 yuan that was judged in the first instance. If you insist on litigation, it will take time, and the final victory is still unknown. If you think that your brother owns an inheritance of 3 million, you should also provide evidence and cannot rely on your empty words. However, Dingbao still did not give a definite indication. The judge then gave her a five-day deadline for her to consider. If she wanted to reconcile, she should submit a letter withdrawing the appeal within the deadline. Otherwise, she should submit a statement within the deadline and invite witnesses to wait for the scheduled hearing. Dingbao heard the instructions and retreated with her husband.

One Piece of Paper as Currency Leads to Severe Punishment

Rice Steward Wrongfully Takes Blame for a Friend

Attorney Li Files an Appeal

Lu Quan, a rice steward at the Lihua Company, was recently involved in an incident. A friend, Tan Hong, was leading a child on Nanjing Road and, due to the heavy traffic, found it inconvenient to cross the street to buy something. He gave Lu Quan a ten-yuan banknote to purchase two dozen cakes and two pounds of bread at Sullivan's. However, the banknote turned out to be counterfeit, and Sullivan discovered it. When asked where he got it, Lu Quan explained that a friend had asked him to buy the items just across the street. Sullivan refused to let Lu Quan leave and, without further explanation, called the police to arrest him. The police handed him over to the First Criminal Court of the Special District Local Court. The court scheduled a hearing for the 18th of last month and appointed Attorney Jin Yu as the pro bono defender. However, Attorney Jin was in Suzhou on business that day and requested Attorney Li Yuan to represent him. Attorney Li reported to the court before the hearing, but the court, without waiting for Attorney Li Yuan to legally appear and defend, directly sentenced Lu Quan to two years and six months of imprisonment, and the counterfeit banknote was confiscated and marked as evidence. It is now reported that the convicted Lu Quan is dissatisfied with the verdict, and Attorney Li, citing Article 306 of the Criminal Procedure Law, argues that the original defender and representative, for the benefit of the defendant, may file an appeal on his behalf. Furthermore, according to the police's indictment, the minimum sentence for the crime is five years or more. Therefore, according to Article 107 of the Criminal Procedure Law, since a defense attorney was appointed by the court, the First Court's verdict without waiting for the attorney to appear and defend is a clear violation of Item 9 of Article 391 of the Criminal Law. It is argued that the appellant's criminal suspicion rests only on one counterfeit banknote, without active proof. Even the police attorney, Ru Bao Yi, argued that the punishment was too severe if treating the offense at its lightest. Therefore, based on these reasons, an appeal has been filed with the Higher Branch Court, requesting that the original judgment be overturned and a new judgment be issued.

Female Worker at Yongan Factory Dies Suddenly, Autopsy Conducted

Yesterday (the 2nd) afternoon at around 5 PM, at the No. 2 Yongan Spinning Factory in Wusong Yunzaobang, a young female worker was found suddenly collapsed at the main entrance behind the factory during the shift dismissal. The gatekeeper immediately reported to Inspector Shi stationed at the factory, who arrived to find her already dead. Her fellow villagers then carried her body to an open space beside the workshop behind. It was discovered that there was a pair of trousers twisted five times around her neck, but not knotted. Yesterday morning, the meal contractor, Zhang Gengquan, filed a report with the First Precinct of the Public Security Bureau, stating: "I, Zhang Gengquan, 38 years old, from Dongyang County, Zhejiang Province, live in workshop number 124 and am a meal contractor. The female worker was brought here by me from my hometown. Her name is Zhang Jingli, 17 years old, also from Dongyang. On the previous day (the 1st), she worked the night shift. The next day, at the end of the shift, she was fined five jiao by foreman Tao Kewei for being lazy. After returning home, the female worker did not eat any porridge or rice all day. After 5 PM, she went out to work at the factory and soon died." Director Zhang Jiguang then went to the scene of the death with the local security officer, Yu Anlian, to inspect the area. He immediately ordered Yu to report to the Shanghai Local Court and request them to send someone to Songjiang to investigate the true cause of death for verification. Because there was no time to report yesterday, the autopsy will likely take place this afternoon.

Old Man Attempts Suicide by Hanging from a Holly Tree

Fortunately Saved by Patrol Police

Yesterday morning around 6 AM, an old man was found hanging himself from a holly tree among the weeds in a deserted grave area west of Jiaotong Road in Zhabei. His body was suspended in the air, a truly terrifying sight. Fortunately, the patrol police of the Third Precinct of the Fourth District spotted him and rushed forward to save him. He had not yet died. They took him to the police station, and after several hours of treatment, he regained consciousness. When questioned by the director, he gave his name as Li Wanghua, 50 years old, from Gong'an County, Hubei Province. He was once a merchant with a wife and children. However, due to financial difficulties, he resolutely left for other provinces to seek work. Unfortunately, after traveling to Shanghai, he not only had nowhere to live but also lacked food and clothing. Now, his pockets were empty, and he had no one to borrow from. With the harsh winter weather, he felt that he would eventually die, so he used his belt to hang himself from the tree. As he spoke, he shed tears of sorrow. The director, seeing his plight as pitiful, ordered him to be sent to the judicial department for further handling.

The Report of the Shanghai Ratepayers' Association on the Audit of the Water Company's Accounts

He De Kui, Pan Xu Lun, and Yu Xi Ji, the three representatives of the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Shanghai Concession, submitted a written report to the association after auditing the accounts of the Water Company as follows: I. Audit Report of the Shanghai Water Company

Section 1: The Origin of the Audit: The Shanghai Public Concession Water Company uniformly increased the water rates for users within the concession by 25% starting in September of this year. The citizens protested, and the undersigned were entrusted by the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Shanghai Concession and the Shanghai Real Estate Association to audit the Water Company's accounts. Starting at the end of September, we went to the company daily to review the account books and registers from 1915 to 1929. Later, the company failed to submit the final accounts for the first half of this year immediately, delaying the process for more than twenty days. The audit is now complete, and the details of the process and the results obtained are reported as follows. (The company's shareholder meeting reports for the last 15 years are attached.)

Section 2: The Reasons Why the Water Company Believes It Should Increase Prices: The Water Company's reasons for increasing prices are that the price of gold has risen, and the annual dividends are calculated in British currency. The amount of silver used to pay dividends has also increased accordingly, and a portion of the various expenses has also increased due to the rise in the price of gold, resulting in the original surplus amount being insufficient for distribution. Therefore, it is necessary to increase prices. The company's capital stock totals £1,163,225, and the fixed annual dividend is £100,020 3s. Currently, calculated at a rate of one shilling sixpence per tael, a total of 1,333,602 taels of silver is required. The estimated income for this year is 2,600,000 taels, and the net profit after deducting all expenses is 689,029 taels. Adding the accumulated surplus of 379,884 taels over the years, the total amount is still 264,689 taels short of the fixed dividend for this year. If this shortfall is extended to next year and added to next year's fixed dividend of 1,333,602 taels (still calculated at a rate of one shilling sixpence per tael), a total of 1,598,291 taels of silver will be required. The estimated income for next year is 2,780,000 taels, and the net profit after deducting all expenses is only 542,000 taels. Using this to pay dividends will result in a significant shortfall of 1,056,291 taels. To make up for this shortfall, the water price must be increased by 30.8% from October of this year to the end of next year. This clause is based on the company's estimate that the dividend is insufficient based on an exchange rate of one shilling sixpence per tael, and the company is trying to find ways to increase revenue. (Note: The Municipal Council has agreed to the Water Company's price increase of 25% from September of this year to the end of next year. If the exchange rate rises to two shillings per tael, the price increase will be reconsidered.) Section 3: Results of the Audit: (1) The benefits obtained by the company's shareholders in the past were overly generous. (2) The current dividend rate of the company has been set by the Municipal Council, that is, its dividends have been guaranteed by the Municipal Council and shall not be reduced. In fact, the benefits obtained by shareholders have not decreased compared with the past, but have been guaranteed. (3) The company's expenses have increased excessively. The above Item 1 has proof from the following facts: (A) The average annual dividend is more than 10%. The following table lists the Class A dividends distributed by the company in the past 15 years:

Year Dividend Bonus Water Supply Extra Benefit Total

(Percent) (Percent) (Percent)

1915 12.00 0.50 12.50

1916 12.00 1.125 13.125

1917 12.00 2.50 14.50

1918 12.00 0.625 12.625

1919 12.50 4.00 17.50

1920 12.50 0.30 13.00

1921 10.00 10.00

1922 7.50 7.50

1923 5.00 5.00

1924 10.00 10.00

1925 10.00 1.25 11.25

1926 10.00 10.00

1927 8.30 1.56 9.86

1928 9.70 1.56 11.26

1929 9.00 1.29 10.29

The average rate for the above 15 years is 11.23%. The average rate for the past 10 years is 9.82%. The average rate for the past 5 years is 10.53%. This is the officially paid dividend and bonus. (B) Distribution of Bonus Shares Twice: The company distributed bonus shares twice in 1921 and 1926 (3,048 shares in 1921, each share at £20, totaling £60,960; 6,706 shares in 1926, each share at £20, totaling £134,120), totaling 9,754 shares, totaling £195,080, accounting for more than 24% of the company's current Class A shares. This bonus share was allocated from the surplus reserve fund and distributed evenly according to the number of shares originally held by the shareholders, without any consideration. Its rights are exactly the same as the originally issued shares. This reserve fund comes from the premiums on previous stock issues, and a portion is from the earnings of previous years. The investor is willing to pay a premium because of (1) the company's excellent reputation, (2) the stability of public utility investment, and (3) the ability to pay high dividends over the years. Once this premium is received, it is the same as the company's ordinary earnings and is indistinguishable from the company's reserve fund. In fact, the stock premium is paid by a portion of new shareholders, and the bonus share is enjoyed equally by old and new shareholders. It is an allocation of earnings and cannot be explained as a return of original capital. There is no doubt about it. Therefore, in addition to the dividends paid annually, the Class A shares also have the benefit of these two lump-sum distributions. Last year, the dividend income of Class A shares was 9% fixed interest and 1.29% bonus, totaling 10.29%. If this 24% bonus share is excluded, the dividend income of the inherited shares is 13.5%, and its benefit is very generous. (C) Distribution of Dividends of Shanghai Water Appliances Limited Company: Before 1926, the company had a department that sold water appliances. Later, the Municipal Council and the company agreed to reorganize the water appliance department separately. The value of all assets in this department, totaling 200,180 taels, was allocated to establish the Shanghai Water Appliances Limited Company, and stocks of the same amount were issued and distributed to the Class A shareholders of the Water Company at that time. The business of the appliance company has developed rapidly in recent years, and the dividends are also quite generous. This is also an additional benefit for the shareholders of the company. To sum up the three points, it is self-evident that the benefits obtained by the company's shareholders in the past were overly generous. The above Item 2 has the following facts to prove: (A) Dividends Allowed by the Municipal Council: The company's current total capital stock is £1,163,215, and the shares are divided into Class A, Class B, and Class C. Class A shares have a par value of £20 each, totaling 40,236 shares, accounting for nearly 70% of the total capital stock. They were issued the earliest, and the benefits are also the most generous. Class B shares were issued after 1926, with a par value of £1 each, totaling 108,505 shares, accounting for nearly 10% of the total capital stock. Class C shares were allowed by the Municipal Council to be issued in 1929, with a par value of £1 each, totaling 250,000 shares, accounting for more than 20% of the total capital stock. In March 1928, the Municipal Council and the company signed a 20-year contract, which stipulates the following regarding dividends: Class A shares are guaranteed 9% interest and can receive bonuses, Class B shares are guaranteed 7% interest and can also receive bonuses, and Class C shares are guaranteed 8% interest and have no bonus rights. The guaranteed interest rate is like this. (B) Bonuses Allowed by the Municipal Council: The contract also stipulates that the water rates collected in the concession must be approved by the Municipal Council. The company is free to set prices for water used by users outside the concession and various ships. The profits obtained by the company from supplying water to users outside the concession and various ships are used to distribute dividends to shareholders, that is, the bonus of Class A and Class B shares mentioned in Item A. This bonus was 1.56% in 1928 and 1.29% in 1929, which is the same for Class A and Class B shares. Therefore, the actual dividend issued for Class A shares is no more than 9%, and the actual dividend issued for Class B shares is more than 7%. In the above two items, the dividends obtained by Class A shares (accounting for 70% of the total shares) in the past two years are as follows:

Year Fixed Interest Bonus (Water Outside Concession) Total Dividend

1928 9.00% 1.56% 10.56%

1929 9.00% 1.29% 10.29%

Note: There is also a 7% dividend to compensate for the shortfall in 1927. The right Class A dividend rate is almost the same as the average rate of 10.67% for the ten years from 1918 to 1927. Compared with the average rate of 9.22% for the five years from 1923 to 1927, it has increased. Moreover, there was no guarantee for the amount of dividends paid by the company in the past. After the contract signed in March 1928, the dividends received by shareholders have an additional guarantee. (C) Dividends of the Water Appliances Limited Company Allowed by the Municipal Council: The stocks of the Water Appliances Company mentioned in Item C of the previous Item 1 were previously issued to the shareholders of the Water Company, and the benefits they receive each year are allowed by the Municipal Council to be distributed as usual. The facts of the above Item 3 are as follows: The amount of water supplied by the Water Company was 10,809,519,328 gallons in 1925 and 13,147,724,477 gallons in 1929. The increase in five years is about 22%. As for the annual expenses, they are shown in the table on the left:

According to the table above, the increase rate of each expense is compared with the increase rate of water output. Except that the increase of water production cost is less, the water delivery cost and management cost are much higher. Furthermore, the rate of increase of certain items of expenses of the company is even greater than this. For example, the amount paid for salaries and wages under the management fee item has the following table from 1925 to this year:

The company's budget for the second half of this year has increased by another 20%. If this budget is implemented, the salary for the second half of this year or next year will increase by three times compared with 1925. Although the salary of some senior employees of the company is calculated in gold pounds and increases according to the exchange rate change, it does not have to be so large. The factory repair and maintenance costs in the following table:

The expenses in 1929 increased by 9 times compared with 1925. During this period, the increase in fixed assets such as houses, machines, and water pipes was only 14%, and the increase in water output was only 22%. As for the impact of the gold-expensive and silver-cheap, the average exchange rate in 1925 was 3 shillings and 1 and a half pence, and the average exchange rate in 1929 was 2 shillings and 4 pence and 19/32. The increase was only 31%, and only a portion of the repair and maintenance costs are affected by the gold price. In addition, the increase in expenses such as the return travel expenses of foreign employees and the miscellaneous expenses of the management office is also very rapid. From this, it can be seen that the company's expenses have increased greatly. Therefore, it is questionable whether the company has done its best to save money.

Section 4: Audit Opinions: (1) According to the above section, the benefits obtained by the company's shareholders in the past and present are too generous. The facts in the past are as above. The current dividend for Class A shares is guaranteed 9% interest, and the bonus for water supply outside the concession is already more than 10%. The dividends of the appliance company and the bonus shares issued in the past are not included. Such a generous dividend is rare for public utilities enjoying a patent. The market price of the company's Class A shares in London this year is about £25, which is 25% higher than the par value. This is clear proof that investors consider the interest rate to be generous. (2) Public utilities should do their best to save on various expenses, because saving one cent reduces the burden on citizens by one cent. In recent years, the company has not been able to practice thrift in terms of expenditure, and has focused on increasing revenue, requesting price increases, which is difficult to satisfy people. (3) The company's estimated total income for this year is 2,600,000 taels, and the dividends to be paid are 1,333,602 taels, accounting for more than 50% of the total water price income. Therefore, more than half of the water price paid by citizens is used for the company to pay dividends. The company's capital stock and dividends must be calculated in British currency. The rise and fall of the gold price are uncertain, and the water price borne by citizens is subject to the risk of changes in the gold price. The annual water price cannot be estimated, and it is necessary to prepare a budget and calculate the loss to citizens based on the gold price, which is detrimental to the interests of citizens and has an impediment. For a fundamental solution, it is necessary to have a comprehensive cost calculation. Report by He De Kui, Pan Xu Lun, and Yu Xi Ji, November 21, 1930.

Free Talk

A Laughing Matter

— Sea Guest

Bank Manager (to his friend): My son swallowed a gold coin, which made everyone extremely anxious.

Friend: Where is he now? Has he been sent to the hospital?

Bank Manager: He was sent to the hospital a long time ago.

Friend: How is it? Has the gold coin come out yet?

Bank Manager: Financial stagnation has not yet been realized.

Customer (seeing two ducks in the duck vendor's basket): How much is one of these ducks?

Duck Vendor: One yuan and four jiao each, two for a total of two yuan and eight jiao. Customer: I only want one, that's enough.

Duck Vendor: No, no, they have to go together.

Customer: You're too inflexible. Why do you insist on people buying two?

Duck Vendor: Because they've been living together for three years. They're a very old couple. I can't bear to break them up.

Manager: Which idiot moved these documents to the bookshelf?

Clerk: Sir, this is where you told me to put them yesterday.

Manager: So, you're calling me an idiot? Fine, you're fired tomorrow.

Driver (to the judge): Your Honor, I was going to sound the horn, but the horn was broken and he couldn't hear it, so I knocked him down.

Judge: Then why didn't you slow down the car or stop it completely?

Driver: Sorry, I didn't think of that.

Jiao Hill Sightseeing Record

— Yue Jiang

On the 29th, Deputy Commander Zhang Xueliang, accompanied by his wife, Ms. Yu Fengzhi, arrived from the capital on the warship "Hai Xing" to visit Jiao Hill. Among those accompanying him were Song Ziwen, Yang Shuzhuang, Hu Ruoyu, and many other important figures. The arrival of these dignitaries added luster to the scenic Jiangshan. The following is a miscellaneous record of the lively events of those few hours, which the reader will surely be pleased to hear.

Cannon Fire in the Thick Fog　News of Deputy Commander Zhang's visit to Jiao Hill was scarcely known beforehand. Around noon, a sudden, resounding cannon fire reverberated, startling the people. Unaware of the details, they ran around spreading the news, inquiring about what had happened. It was then learned that the Xiangshan Fort was firing cannons in salute to Deputy Commander Zhang. At the time, thick fog covered the Yangtze River, and it was unknown that the "Hai Xing" warship had already docked near Jiao Hill.

Many Dignitaries at Jiao Hill　Before Mr. Zhang's arrival, Chairman Ye and the heads of various departments had already taken the "Da Ya" patrol ship to Jiao Hill to await his arrival. Jiao Hill is located far in the heart of the river, and visitors often found it difficult to cross the water, so it was usually rarely visited, and felt desolate and quiet, indeed showing its deep mountain nature. This time, with the concentration of military and political dignitaries, the famous temple attracted more visitors than ever before, and Jiao Hill truly became a lively hill.

The Monks Extremely Busy　The lunch was originally ordered from the Meili Society Western restaurant by the provincial government, but because many found it unappetizing and not in line with the characteristics of Jiao Hill, and unsuitable to adorn the scenic spot, it was changed to a vegetarian meal of five tables prepared by the Dinghui Temple itself. The monks were already extremely busy pouring tea and water, and then they began to prepare the vegetarian meal, working hastily to meet the overwhelming demand.

Gifts and Requests from the Monks　After lunch at the Zhenjiang Pavilion, the abbot, Ji Tang, led the group on a tour of various places, explaining the various historical sites in detail, and presented various rubbings from stone inscriptions as gifts. Mr. Zhang accepted them all to keep as mementos. The abbot also presented a scroll, requesting Mr. Zhang to inscribe it. He immediately wrote the four characters "(Justice and Righteousness Endure)," and signed it "Zhang Xueliang." The brushstrokes were vigorous and full of heroic spirit, truly befitting a general. After the tour, Mr. Zhang immediately ordered his staff to give 1,000 yuan to support the temple, and awarded 200 yuan to the provincial government's guard team, and 100 yuan to the provincial government's military band, totaling no less than 1,400 or 1,500 yuan.

Wu Zhihui's Portrait and Poem

— Yan Yun

The articles of the famous figure of the Party and State, Mr. Wu Zhihui, use simple language to convey profound truths, and his eloquence is known throughout the world. However, his poems are rarely circulated. This April, Xu Beihong of Yixing created an oil painting of him, about three feet high, full of spirit and vigor. It was Beihong's most satisfying portrait to date, and was reproduced in the National Day Pictorial of the News. Mr. Wu cherished it greatly, and wrote a recent poem in seal script, "Visiting Xie Gong Pier," to thank Beihong. He also had the portrait made into a three-color print, the size of a quarto page. Whenever friends asked for his calligraphy, he would leave a corner of the left side vacant for pasting the image. Chen Zhenru, Yang Xingfo, and Li Xiaosheng have all received such gifts, making it a unique combination of calligraphy and painting. Recently, I saw him write a seven-character quatrain and calligraphy it to present to the Minister of Interior, Niu Tisheng, along with a long postscript and a photograph. The poem reads: "(Sharing a dormitory, we responded to the imperial examination back then, our heroic spirits unmatched. Leaning on the window, the Qinhuai River remains as before, only we gaze at each other with whitened hair.)" It is said that Niu and Mr. Wu were old friends from forty years ago, having taken the autumn imperial examination together and entered the Nanjing Academy together. Recently, they came to Beijing and lived together again on the banks of the Qinhuai River. (Recompense)

Further Research on the Lyrics of "Yu Tang Chun"

— Tianxu Wosheng

Last Tuesday, the "Free Talk" section published "Research on the Lyrics of 'Yu Tang Chun'," stating that "there is no example of 通 [tōng] (to understand) as a homophone for 臣 [chén] (subject)." In my opinion, rhyme schemes in lyrics and musical compositions naturally arise, and the three hundred poems of the Book of Songs do not adhere to pre-existing rhyme schemes to restrict later generations. Those who specialize in the language of the rulers of past dynasties but use their personal habits to judge music, will thus deem things to be "non-standard." Therefore, scholars with broad knowledge cite ancient texts as evidence, pointing out that there have been predecessors. For example, Tao Qian's drinking, or the many cases in "Forest of Grotto Immortals" are innumerable. Poetry and lyrics are like that, much less the performance of dramas! Whether they gain wide support with the masses is beyond whether or not something is right or wrong. The so-called "zhe [轍]" in Peking Opera is like speaking of something having tracks to follow. The so-called "tracks" are the traces of wheels. If there has never been a road before, then there are no tracks to follow, and not conforming to the tracks is the same as not conforming to the proper path. Mr. Ling Sheng's name is Ping [屏] (screen) in Mandarin, but is pronounced geng [庚] (seventh celestial stem) and qing [青] (blue/green) in local dialects. Mao Xihe once used the rhyme of "peng meng [烹萌]" to rhyme with "peng meng [蓬蒙]," likely using the sounds of his own local dialect to force the rhyme to achieve his goal of breaking boundaries. But in reality, "peng meng [烹萌]" can both be read as open-mouth sounds, like "bang mang [傍茫]", then why can't it rhyme with "jiang yang [江陽]"? Therefore, following Xihe's theory, nearly all sounds of rhymes can be rotated. Calling something that goes "south by driving the chariot north", which is basically to turn things back to front and make it the other way around. We can not speak of praise or criticism of it. The sound values geng qing [庚青] and zhen wen [眞文] and yuan gu [元古] all communicated in their earlier days, so if east winter [東冬] can be in harmony with geng qing [庚青], then rotating to zhen wen yuan [眞文元] naturally has examples that can be referred to. Therefore, the word "gen [根]" in the text below is not strange. However, such as "jin xin yin [金心陰]" belong to the rhyme value of qin [侵], that is, the closed-mouth rhyme value. Musical rules of the song consider that originally there was no borrowing examples for wu tou [務頭] of the past! Even though Mr. Xuan has claims for some aspects of the matter, in the end it is not publicly accepted. The flaw of the lyric in "Yu Tang Chun" is that the words "jin xin yin [金心陰]" and their cohort can not harmonize, but this isn't so for hong tong long [紅桐龍] and their cohort. Because the rhyme of qin [侵] doesn't harmonize with dong dong [東冬], so actually there isn't a trail to follow. Only when the singer is very unaware of there being trouble, so that the listener feels that the change happens very smoothly and with proper inflections. Only for hong tong long [紅桐龍] is it a nasal sound, and it isn't yin [陰] and is yang [陽], and one feels pushed and not accepted, giving listeners an unpleasant experience. That Yanqiu's changes to two rhymes for ren chen are pretty close to satisfying people's feelings, and that Shaoqing said there aren't any suitable edits to Hong Tong and only to keep this one flaw actually feels like a pity! I mean that for the words dao hong tong [到洪桐], the word dao can be shortened and used as a filler word, and by reading the two characters hong tong in sequence, what is below them, such as the one character cheng, they become well rounded on the sound and tone, what do you think about that? As for the "alliance pledge" segment, then Yanqiu's lyrics aren't as good as those of Huisheng, so later scholars should choose the better parts and discard the rest. Furthermore, such as the jade cup, it originally isn't for hitting, but changing the character hit to the character place, then it can work, and it is more proper than buy! Trays made from blue jade can be changed to flower vases. The character flower doesn't stand out, and it isn't enough to show its extravagance, so it would be better to keep it the same! And for the three hundred liang being changed to one hundred liang, the original three hundred liang is more of a figure of speech, and one hundred is the exact number and feels unnecessary. Because if forget eight procuress gets a peck of gold, but when meeting (a client), they still need three hundred, and if the matchmaker is only getting one hundred, then that is too little. I hope to pose these questions to Shaoqing to know his opinions.

Shao Lou's Recording Record

— Liang

Wang Shaolou amazed Shanghai with his debut, and now he has returned home with a reputation. Before his departure, the Greater China Record Company invited him to record five records. At that time, Shaolou was performing his farewell performances, and it seemed difficult to manage his voice for recording at the same time. However, that was not the case. Judging from the first day's recording of "Fa Men Si" (The slow Xipi tune of 塢縣 is fresher than that of Ju Peng. The entire segment is without any flaws or reservations, and is especially valuable) and the "Visiting Mother" segment (The đoạn (section) of (未開言) has not been spoken; a section of the quick ban (clapper accompaniment) from a loud shout (separations from brothers) and (有○賢弟) two sentences of shaking board are all included without omissions (Brothers) is where places lift and fall and is heroic simple and Su (Jun) Shaoqing is saying that it has been more than a decade since this inspiring phrase was heard), "Zhan Taiping" (A cannon sound like to the segment of Xipi shaking board that has baby腔 (baby sound) and 嘎調 (gā diào) and crying voice and higher and lower tones so all must be complete, and now there are few who can have this play so to see that one can hear this sound and have the vocal cords that rare). The two sections from (千歲爺) to (old man is willing to die and is unwilling to end) are a flowing board and shaking board and crying voice and following board is sweet and pleasing), and the second day's recording of the "Zhuo Fang" segment (A bright moon is a segment that Shaoqing said both has the merits of Tan Yu's speech and is full of song feeling and it belongs to a knowing speech) Bao Lian Deng segment (I should be a segment of Erhuang Yuanban (original rhythm) and this section hasn't yet been recorded and it is a red play and it is expected that it will be very popular in this trip south) Fa Chang Huan Zi (Because of Xue's home is connect to the reversal of Erhuang's three eyes and this is the true transmission of Yu (Shuyan) stream, this play is externally seen as simple but internally its difficulty is being stable and well received and this has become the most popular new style singing play), not only are the sounds as round and bright as usual, but they are also able to last, showing the hard work he put in during his throat rest. Shaolou's singing style resembles Shu Yan, praised both in the north and south. Therefore, the success of these five records is a foregone conclusion. It is also heard that the Great China's recording this time used the latest technology (the engineer just returned from an inspection in the United States last week). When the records are sold in half a month, the center circle of the record cover will also be improved, and the gloss of the records will also be enhanced. This is truly a good phenomenon in the promotion of national goods.

Travels in Southeast Asia (90)

— Ling Hua

On the sixth, a friend talked about the customs of Myanmar, where men and women of the lower class are very free in marriage, with hardly any wedding ceremony. This reminded me of the verse in the Book of Songs, "You come with your carts, I will move with your gifts." Before arriving in Myanmar, some said that this place had a Yin-Yang sect that worshiped the male genitals, hanging them on the doors of houses to show the public. Upon arriving here, I asked Master Wan, who said that this place was influenced by India, but this sect had not yet reached Myanmar, but was still in India. The sect uses the male genitals as "I" and the female genitals as "Dao," combining them as "I enter Dao," which is a kind of sexual religious force that is very powerful. Every festive season, they hold large gatherings, where even elders, seniors, and distinguished scholars dress up in various guises and perform dances to offer to the goddess and seek her favor for blessings and love. He also said that Brahmanism has a special ritual, where those who study in India and live in the homes of masters know that before men and women engage in intercourse, they must have their children undress and the man respectfully bow to them before engaging in sexual activity. At first, I found it strange, but later I understood its religious meaning. I laughed and said that in today's world, the customs of overthrowing religion and etiquette have become the norm, and there is no longer any respect for elders or teachers. In the future, people will only worship money and women, and I fear that this sect will flourish in the world.

On the seventh, I am now studying the alms bowl entrusted by the Burmese monks. At first, I thought it was made of pottery, and if it were mixed with various dishes of food, it would become a confused mess. But upon closer inspection, it is not made of pottery but of a porcelain-like material. It is slightly similar to Fujian lacquerware with extremely intricate patterns, varying in size and very lightweight. It has a lid and contains several small foreign boxes that can hold various items, making it very suitable for household use as well. Generally, the alms begging is done by novice monks, with the whole temple's monks taking turns to do the work. It is usually held in the right hand, but some are tied with a strap and hung from the shoulder. As for the junior monks, some carry umbrellas, while others do not, and there are reasons to inquire about this. Generally, those with higher qualifications are allowed to carry umbrellas, while novice monks are not allowed to carry umbrellas, and they must endure rain and wind on their heads, walking barefoot in the water, assimilating with nature and practicing hardship. Moreover, many of the young monks are children from wealthy families sent to the temple to study and become monks, and many are nobles. Like Ananda, who went begging for alms, they should not be underestimated, for the Burmese people consider monks to be their teachers in morality and learning.

Warmth in the Heart (328)

— Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Sixteen:　Cuixiu Earnestly Asks for Words from the Teacher　Generous Discussions of Military Affairs at a Brothel Feast for Heroines

Ye Haoran said, "We shouldn't just listen to the opera next door. We came here to fill our stomachs, so let's not forget our purpose. First, let's order food. You guys should call for some lively music, and at the same time, write out the song list. We need to arrange the collaborations and not waste any time." Long Ziyun said, "Not wrong. We came here to fulfill the Tang Dynasty poet's lines, the so-called 'green ant newly brewed wine, small red clay stove.' And it just so happens that it's very cold tonight, so we must have Cantonese hot pot." At this time, the waiter had already placed a white notebook and a pencil from behind his ear on the table, and also brought over the menu printed by their Xinghua Restaurant. Besides this, there was also a list of what fresh dishes were available at different market prices, which was available in each room. Ye Haoran held the pencil and said, "Hot pot is a must. Let's have a two-dollar hot pot. Besides that, what other dishes do you want?" Everyone then ordered a chaotic mess of conch, pigeon pine, fragrant mushrooms, and black bean chicken. Lin Zifan then took on the task of writing the song list, as he knew exactly who to call for and who to sit next to, as if he had an account in his stomach. Before long, a red clay stove, steaming hot, was brought up, along with a large platter with ten dishes of raw meat, raw fish, raw chicken, and raw shrimp. The ten dishes were different. Besides this, there was also a large basket of spinach, as well as lard, wine, and soy sauce, everything you could want. Zuo Shichen said, "In winter, you should eat that kind of thing. I remembered the snowy scenery of cutting off bloody meat in the Dream of the Red Chamber, but unfortunately, Shanghai doesn't have that snowy scenery." Long Ziyun said, "Then you also need a group of girls like Shi Xiangyun to personally cook it to have the same feel." Lin Zifan said, "If we go to Six Three Pavilion in Hongkou to eat beef, there are Japanese women who will personally cook for us." Long Ziyun said, "The maids in Japanese restaurants, called '酌婦' in Japanese, are very elegant. Don't underestimate them. Many of them have graduated from advanced elementary school, and there are even female students from middle school." Ling Zhixiang said, "When will we go to Hongkou for a meal? Before, because we couldn't communicate with them, it felt a bit awkward. Now that we have Mr. Ye Haoran as a translator, it shouldn't be awkward." Ye Haoran said, "Okay, one day I'll treat everyone to go." Just as he was saying that, A Su came in with Yuan Jing's song. She only heard the words "treat" and said, "Young Master Ye is going to treat? Is it at Sister A Xing's place?" Long Ziyun laughed and said, "Young Master Ye said the treat is at a Japanese restaurant in Hongkou, not in a brothel. He wants to invite you to go together." A Su said, "Oh, is it at a Japanese restaurant? Then thank you. I don't care about other things, but we have to take off our shoes and walk in our socks, which is a bit too much to handle."

Cotton Yarn Market Weak in the Morning, Strong in the Afternoon

The yarn market fell in the morning and fluctuated in the afternoon, with the overall trend remaining weak. Actual sales were unusually sluggish. There was no demand for spot yarn from any party, so inventory was gradually increasing. Most retail investors showed considerable anxiety. The attitude of the Chaozhou merchants remained calm. Spot yarn sales in the market were stagnant. With the Lunar New Year approaching, all parties were in the process of closing accounts. There was little hope at present, so most people had a pessimistic outlook.

Tiao Biao (Trademarks) results were strong. The Tiao Biao market opened higher due to the rise in American cotton, and retail investors resisted short positions, causing the market to rise slightly by two or three points. Due to a lack of buyers in the market, selling pressure suddenly increased, and the market suddenly fell, resulting in a drop of 467. In the afternoon, the Tiao Biao yarn market was stimulated by news that factories were maintaining high prices, and buying interest surged again. Each month's prices increased by an average of one, two, or three qian. The total transaction volume for the day was 29,150 bales. Sellers included Chang 1,750 bales, Dachangcheng 1,000 bales, Gongtai 850 bales, Senkang 1,400 bales, and the remaining sellers at 600 to 700 bales. Buyers included 1,950 bales, Yichang 1,100 bales, Dafeng 1,600 bales, and the remaining buyers at 300, 500, 600, and 700 bales. The closing prices are recorded on the left.

Cotton Market Remains Firm

The cotton market remained firm, with American cotton rising again. However, there were no transactions for spot cotton from various factories. In reality, the market remained flat. However, the supply of Han cotton remained scarce, and some buyers held tight, refusing to release it. If supplies from various parties could be plentiful in the future, changes would be observed at that time. Currently, the market remained in a fluctuating state.

Han Biao was high. The Han Biao market opened higher in the morning, following the rise in foreign cotton by one or two qian. The market closed flat, with near months rising by one qian and far months flat. In the afternoon, the yarn market rose again, and sentiment tightened, leading to stronger buying interest and some covering of short positions. Prices for each month rose by one or two qian. Grain Rice Market Reaches Peak, Large Scale Selling

Due to the end of the lunar calendar year, sales become increasingly sluggish.

Yesterday, about sixty ships from the inland arrived in Zhabei. The amount of goods transported by machines for various factories in Luli also increased significantly. As a result, the inventory in this port increased daily. Due to the upcoming closure of accounts at the end of the lunar calendar year, most people adopted a wait-and-see attitude and focused on collecting debts. Consequently, the market sales became stagnant, and prices continued to fall. High-quality Taibai Japonica rice was in short supply, with prices dropping by several cents. The price of high quality outside Thirteen yuan and eight cents. The price of Zhongguan Japonica rice gradually fell by fourteen cents. Ordinary Japonica rice only held at the Eleven yuan mark. However, the future remains uncertain. Arrivals of unhusked rice were slow, and sales were sluggish, continuing to decline by two cents. Both Yangxian and Duxian rice declined by half a cent, with the Xian rice market also trending softer. Even the retail sales in the port area were silent. High quality rice was barely holding at Eleven yuan and seven cents. Wholesale transactions were declining, and buying interest was unusually quiet. All shifts in sentiment led to further declines, dropping by four cents. High-quality wholesale rice was priced at thirteen yuan and six or seven cents, now below cost. Customer sales were not progressing, with only a few shops inquiring. The price of Yinyuan topped rice was slightly lower due to its scarcity. The price of medium quality declined slightly by three cents. The overall situation was very weak.

In the southern part of Shanghai, over thirty ships arrived from the lower reaches of the river yesterday. After several days of repairs, the roads have become slightly more active. Regular transactions and Suzhou used the same machinery. Due to the falling prices of goods, customers from the surrounding countryside preferred to purchase mid-to-high quality rice, but the prices declined by one or two cents. Top quality sold for Thirteen yuan and six cents, and transactions were small and sporadic. Southern merchants sold green glutinous rice and Songjiang Jia rice, but there was actually no one asking about the origins. The market gradually declined by a little more than two cents. The top market price opened at Eleven yuan and two cents. The trend for sheep tip rice was slightly weak, while Dujian still had customers buying, so the price declined by a cent. Top quality Dujian still required eleven yuan and eight or nine cents. Sales of ordinary Bianyinyuan rice were consistently slow, with prices falling by four or five cents, indicating a significantly weakened situation. Although the decline of rice prices here was more moderate compared to Zhabei, the overall trend remains downward.

Flour Market Has Stabilized

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning and afternoon, prices for each month had stabilized because foreign price quotations recovered a good two, four, five cents. And the domestic situation is based on this kind of price as if it would be difficult to be more economical and the manufacturer's current prices and futures are completely different. The fact that spot goods are not surging smoothly is recognized by the public, but although the weakness of futures is mostly due to the environment, customer merchants' skepticism and suspicion is also the main reason for the weakness of futures. If customer merchants do not consider market prices but aim to receive goods, then at a minimum a standard situation can be maintained to a great extent. But now, customer merchants have gradually paid attention to the recent recovery, which is expected to be the reason. As a result, the current month was up by one fen and two li and a half, the first month up by one fen and two li and a half, February up by one fen and three li, March up by two li and a half, April up by five li, and May was unchanged.

Futures and Spot Wheat Both Enter a Silent State

Yesterday, after the opening of the wheat market in the morning and afternoon, the market for each month was generally stagnant. Because foreign price quotations rose slightly, speculative sellers naturally ceased activity. At this point, the bottom of the market was completely influenced by foreign countries. If the domestic situation were considered, it would be unexpected. However, there was still a tendency for the prices of far-term months to recover. As a result, the prices for the current month and the first month were unchanged, the second month down by a small one fen, three li, the third/fourth months down by two fen, and May was unchanged. The spot wheat market remained silent. The factories in this port did not receive any news of foreign wheat assistance. The city only sold 200 packs of Kaiwan wheat, with the price being as low as four liang and two fen. It was purchased by Wusong Hefeng.

The Oil Market: White Tung Oil is Flourishing

Jingzhou oil will arrive in mid-month... This train of oil continues to arrive in Shanghai.

The foreign sales of white tung oil are gradually showing signs of activity after a period of stagnation. Shengli Yanghang and others continue to show interest in spot goods, but due to the strict price limits, daily transactions are only a few dozen tons. After the opening of the overseas sales price at sixteen liang and four qian, it has already risen to seventeen liang. Due to the difficulty in improving domestic sales, the wholesale price has been hovering around the fifteen liang mark. With customer goods arriving sporadically from the source, the asking price for Xiangtong oil has been raised by one qian to fifteen liang and three qian, showing a rather strong trend.

The new stock of asphalt is expected to arrive in Hancheng around the middle of this month. The stock of Macheng oil is dwindling daily. Small quantities are sold at seventeen liang and four qian. Premium quality oil still requires seventeen liang and eight qian. Although trains from the interior have continued to arrive in Shanghai in recent days, the numbers are very small, and most of them are transit goods.

This factory's cloth. Yesterday, fine cloth was slightly better. After the price reduction, the dyeing route was quickly activated. Yanghe rose by two and a half fen, and Laba Tong Caiqiu also hardened slightly. Fine twill fell again. Blue Shuangyu fell by a small five fen. Yanghe and Jincheng fell by two and a half fen, actually because spot goods were flooding the market. The sales trend of coarse cloth and lower-quality goods was smoother. Yesterday, Ningbo, Shantou, Xiamen, and other merchants added purchases. The demand on this street was also strong, so nine-pound cloth all required four liang and two qian, which was very firm. Lower-Grade Yarn Overcoats Sell Slowly, Prices Fall

Women's Colored Overcoats Particularly Active

The sales prices of low-end yarn and overcoat fabrics priced at 1.4 to 1.5 qian have been falling in recent days. Hualun Yongfeng goods, which initially sold for 1.5 qian, fell again to 1.1 qian, 7 fen, 5 li, and even 4 li. This is because sales are slow and stagnant, and the goods purchased by various firms previously have not been sold. Zhaofeng and Madasheng yarn overcoats were reduced to 1.2 qian and 5 fen yesterday.

The sales momentum of women's colored overcoat fabrics has been better this year than last year, leading to a sudden surge in the price of raw materials. Sales of red, yellow, green, gray, and mixed colors have been brisk, and prices have firmed up, especially for jacquard and printed yellow-brown fabrics, which are particularly rare and popular. Women's clothing stores on this street are mostly offering high prices to buy them. Plain, unpatterned fabrics of ordinary brands are generally sold for 3 liang, 2 qian, 5 fen to 3 liang, 7 qian, and 8 fen.
