Shanghai News

Business News

The Ford Motor Company announced that it is currently showing sound films about its car factories on roads throughout the United States. People who have not had the opportunity to tour the Ford factories can see various aspects of Ford's car manufacturing. The film includes several coal mines owned by Ford, which supply the coal used. Ford also has iron mines that extract pig iron for use. Various materials are transported by Ford's own ships to Dorset Bin to manufacture cars. All important aspects of car manufacturing are included, and everything is explained with sound. Ford's iron foundries, large copper factories, coke ovens, and machine shops use machines instead of manual labor, which is also included in the film. It is very interesting and informative. Thousands of cars are manufactured every day, so each part must be extremely precise in order to be installed without delay. This aspect is also explained in the film. The manufacturing of each part is accurate to one-thousandth of an inch. In the Ford factory, all materials and parts are transported to various locations using vehicles that operate on a fixed schedule. Many vehicles travel on large steel cables, carrying white-hot iron ingots to the iron foundry. The film also shows how by-products are used to produce gas, carbon dioxide, and pharmaceuticals. The first Ford road show started several months ago and was very successful. Now, the film will be shown in smaller cities, with special parts available for people to view and supplement the film. The items are transported by a fleet of Ford trucks and come equipped with screens.

The Lincoln Motor Company announced that the first time it delivered to Dallas and Fort Worth, there was a seven-seater sedan called Lincoln Second, which was the second car manufactured by the Lincoln Motor Company factory. Currently, the Lincoln Second car's engine is undamaged and is still being used by the management office that bought the car, White-Legette Motor Company, to promote business. This car has a long history and has traveled the equivalent of seven times around the earth. However, the car body is still strong and durable. When this car first arrived in Texas, it immediately underwent testing to check all road conditions. It traveled 40,000 miles in six months. Later, General Aielu of Qingye saw that it was smooth to drive and had a strong body, so he paid to buy it. He used it until his death. After that, the car was bought back by the management office and is currently in someone's hands. According to the latest calculations, this special car has traveled 144,945 miles, of which 40,000 miles were traveled by General Aielu. The repair cost was less than 50 US dollars.

The Wella Company at the corner of Nanjing Road and Sichuan Road announced that because the Christmas holiday is coming soon, it is expected that all sectors will purchase large quantities of gifts. To thank customers for their patronage throughout the year, all women's clothing, such as various silks, gold and silver silk, and velvet, will be discounted to 75% off, and even half off. In addition, the company's new variety of new and ingenious toys, more than 3,000 types of all sizes are on display for all to visit.

The Zhongxi Pharmacy General Store on Fourth Road announced that it is now the time for all men and women to nourish themselves during the winter season. It is also the time to promote the national calendar and settle accounts in advance this year. With few days left in the year, the pharmacy has a large stock of goods and will display various goods in full supply. The two branches in Zhejiang Road and Xiaodongmen Central Nanshi will also hold a winter sale for 20 days. In addition to reducing prices and selling at discounts, there are also valuable gifts such as perfume, honey, hundred flower essence, fragrant powder, and Xiaoguniang Xuehua. There is also a movie ticket, which is scheduled to start on December 5th of the national calendar.

He once invented the Yan script to distinguish the seal script of past dynasties. He studied the original character and its original meaning. The strokes are divided into Yan Shang and Yan Xia, and the meaning of seal script is included in the Li, Cao, and Zhen scripts. Therefore, he wrote "The Origin of Characters", a circulation consultation of one hundred and twenty volumes, which has long been deeply appreciated by Zhang Se'an of Nantong, Sha Jian'an of Rugao, and Jin Hengwei of the same county. Youth Zone

Opening of the Girls' Dormitory at Great China University

— Zexiang

Opening the girls' dormitory has become a common practice at various universities in this port. Our Great China University's girls' dormitory has long been known as the "West Palace," so of course it's no exception. The opening event has been held several times. This term, the student union also sent a letter to the girls' student association asking them to choose a date for the opening in order to carry out a cleaning campaign. According to the reply from the girls' student association, the girls' dormitory will be open from 9:00 am to 4:00 pm on November 26th. At the same time, the girls' student association also posted a notice in the girls' dormitory stating that the dormitory will be open on November 26th and that the students are requested to decorate and tidy up their rooms slightly to make them clean and attractive. So the female students were busy tidying up and arranging things, and the male and female students were busy repairing their clothes. From 9:00 am to 4:00 pm on that day, the students on the campus road kept coming and going. Inside the dormitory, male and female students were chatting and laughing, and some were preparing fruits and refreshments for their best friends. This grand occasion came to an end in the evening.

Record of the Opening of Qunying Residence

— Wu

The Women's Dormitory of Great China University was Opened on November 26th

Since the beginning of autumn, the women's dormitories of various universities have been opened one after another. The women's dormitory of Great China University is naturally no exception. Speaking of the women's dormitory of Great China University, when it was first located on Jiaozhou Road, it was named "West Palace," as if it were in opposition to the "East Palace" of Fudan University. It had been opened twice. This autumn, the new campus of Great China University in Fanwangdu was completed, and a new women's dormitory was built. It faces the Xizhe River and the Liwa and Lida Villages to the west, and the Suzhou River can be seen to the south. To the east are the Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway and the campus of St. John's University. In this environment, the school authorities named it "Qunying Residence." Readers should not confuse this with "Junfang Residence" or "Qunfang Gathering," as that would be insulting and disrespectful to our female palace masters. Looking at the entire campus, the women's dormitory is located to the south, so it could also be called "South Palace." However, this name is not very common, so we can still use the name "West Palace."

The opening hours were from 9:00 AM to 11:30 AM and from 1:00 PM to 5:00 PM on the 26th. Those who had never entered the palace gates were generally amazed and rushed there, so the road leading to Qunying Residence was filled with male students, resembling the grand scene of "Shanyin Road." In front of the palace, there is a winding stream spanned by a wooden bridge. Some say that this bridge can be called the "Magpie Bridge," but Qixi (Double Seventh Festival) has already passed. Some say that this bridge is the boundary between male and female students and can be named the "Yin-Yang Bridge." In my opinion, for friends who are heartbroken, this bridge can also be called the "Bridge of Helplessness." After crossing the bridge, you pass through a road lined with ancient cypresses and holly trees. (The current situation) After walking only a dozen steps, you arrive at the palace gate.

Upon entering the palace gate, on one side is the gatehouse, and directly ahead is the reception room. Curtains hung on the side by the window, and large printed screens hung on the side by the corridor. Within this area, several rattan tables and bamboo chairs are scattered for receiving guests. Their usual reception hours stop at 9:00 PM, and most visitors come in the evening. At that time, the lights are dim and the conversation is soft, perhaps for which the printed curtains are set up.

On the day of the opening, the Women's Student Union assigned six hostesses to each floor. The route was up the left and down the right. On the bottom floor, to the left is the kindergarten, and to the right are the dining hall and reading room, which are not worth our attention. We still want to see the dormitories on the second and third floors. The arrangement of their dormitories, from the surface, is better than that of the male students. Each room houses two people. Upon entering, there are two wardrobes built into the wall on the west side of the door, providing them with space to store clothes. Each person also has a desk, a bed, and an orange crate. Because each person's aesthetic is different, the arrangements are also different. The rooms of students in the kindergarten teacher training class generally have many figures and drawings of arts and crafts. The rooms of female students who are good at socializing have many of their own photographs. The rooms of female students who believe in Christianity have pictures of the Virgin Mary hanging. Other rooms also have wallpaper or Western paintings. In terms of books, the female students who study hard generally have more books than others, perhaps because they were all tidied up for the opening. Each person has a steel-framed bed with wooden slats. The decorations and bedding are generally white, but there are also other colors. The orientation of the beds depends on each person's arrangement, but there are a few beds that are connected, which is probably an exception. (The women's dormitory is U-shaped, with the opening facing south. The rooms facing south are filled with sunlight, and because of the decorations, they are more beautiful and clean than the rooms facing the shade.)

The above is generally the common situation. The following few items are roughly the anecdotes I saw.

In a room on the left corner of the third floor, the room with windows on two sides is very clean. Their beds are combined into one bed, with two snow-white pillows placed on one side, embroidered with the red words "Sweet Dream." I think they must be hoping to have fantastical and sweet dreams every night.

On the second floor, a sunny room is decorated with pink paper window curtains. A female student from Guangdong used red bed sheets, and a framed photograph of a knot is placed on the table, probably of a newlywed, which is very noteworthy.

At the head of one female student's bed was placed a large foreign doll, which was very cute. I don't know if this foreign doll is a representative of her own children, used to comfort loneliness or express maternal love.

A certain Miss is a foreign girl at Great China University. She pays attention to her appearance and decorations. She usually perms her hair, and her eyes are dyed with ambiguous colors. She wears Western clothes and long stockings and high heels, which always attracts attention. Some say she is like a social butterfly. On the day of the opening, she wore a green cheongsam and greeted guests at the door. In her room, there are many small portraits of this lady. When we walked out of the room, we praised her a few times, and she responded with a slight smile.

Many female students prepared many refreshments in their rooms, probably to entertain good friends. I accepted their kindness in a certain lady's room and tasted some chocolates and bananas, etc. However, many female students gave male students the cold shoulder (especially in the afternoon), perhaps because their lovers had come to their rooms or for other unspeakable pain, and they closed the door.

The names of palace master and queen have been rarely mentioned since they were banned. It is said that Great China University used to have a Zhang (name not mentioned), but unfortunately she has left her alma mater with a square cap. This autumn, the patriotic female poet came to Great China University but is said to have withdrawn from her grade due to academic performance (?). For the time being there is no queen or palace master. Miss Elizabeth P., who is usually praised, is living a lonely life this autumn, and the arrangement of her room is exceptionally simple, which is very disappointing to us.

The opening of the women's dormitory was originally scheduled for four days, but it was later reduced to one day. However, even within this one day, there were twists and turns. As far as I know, some ladies' photos were taken away, and many ladies' perfume bottles, handkerchiefs, fountain pens, and packages were gone. Furthermore, the fruit plates and cups arranged on the tables were in a mess, and some ladies' private letters (…?) disappeared without a trace. As a result, the ladies' public anger was stirred. Originally, it was prepared not to be opened in the afternoon, but later it was guaranteed by Chairman Hua Yu and personally monitored in the dormitory, like Siamese soldiers. In reality, most of the doors were closed, and those who came later did not have much to see. The male students taking things was probably driven by curiosity and caused a funny incident. This short piece is just to let everyone know the living situation of female students and the pranks of male students, so the content is very simple, like the falling flowers and flowing water of the late spring.

Great China University Faculty and Student Talk

— You Pei

The Great China University Student Union held a discussion meeting in classroom No. 212 of the school at 7:00 PM the other day, inviting representatives of the school affairs council, representatives of the mass education committee, and all members of the various departments and colleges. Those who attended included Principal Ou Yuanhuai, Dean of Academic Affairs Lu Jizeng, Director of General Affairs Wu Haoran, Dean Sun Lei, Chairman of the Mass Education Committee Yu Zhihan, and all executive committee members of the student unions of various departments and colleges, totaling about one hundred people. Seven bells rang to announce the start of the meeting. First, Xu Zexiang, Chairman of the Student Union, gave an opening speech, briefly stating that the school's history is only six years old, and that it has achieved such rapid progress in this very short period of time. Others find it strange, but in fact, this is the inevitable result of our faculty and students working together. If there were no three hardships of those who run the school working hard, teachers teaching hard, and students studying hard, there would be no development today. Today, we can hold a meeting in this magnificent new school building, and everyone naturally feels twelve points of comfort in their hearts. The reason why the Student Union invited all of you teachers and students today is, on the one hand, for a reunion, and on the other hand, because we have had such rapid development in the past year, and we also hope to have even faster progress in the coming year. However, the people who bear this responsibility are of course the School Affairs Council and the Student Union, which are relatively important. However, I and a few other members of this Student Union have very weak abilities. In the future, how can we directly increase the interests of students and open up the development of school affairs? All of this depends on the guidance of all of you teachers and students, etc. Then, Principal Ou Yuanhuai and Dean of Academic Affairs Lu Jizeng gave speeches in succession. Next, representatives from various departments and colleges gave speeches and work reports until after 9:00 PM when the meeting adjourned.
